However, the Communist Party should maintain the right to lead various movements, and should still occupy the leading position in collective combinations. (2) The organization of the Third International should be adapted to local needs according to local conditions. The Communist Parties of various countries should enjoy broad autonomy, but they are still subject to the control of the Third International and continue to be guided by the Third International. 3. Communist Parties of various countries should assume special tasks separately according to the needs of various countries. For example, in China, they should focus on opposing the aggression of foreign imperialism and defending the integrity of Chinese territory. In France, they should engage in more extensive actions, such as winning over the masses, resisting Fascism, and promoting Franco-Russian cooperation. 'In the Czech Republic, the recent accusations by Communist Party members that President Masaryk and Foreign Minister Benes have fascist tendencies should be corrected.'" (Havas, 28th)

American Writer Endures Hardship, Crosses the Alps on an Elephant

Turin, Italy The American writer Harry Burton, who endured hardship to cross the Alps, arrived here leisurely on the back of an elephant, signifying the end of his entire journey. The giant elephant "Miss Dolly" still has sore feet. After entering the city, children fed it fodder, which it swallowed very quickly, even chewing the newspapers wrapping the fodder. The writer and his party will take a train back to Paris tomorrow. (Havas, 28th)

Former Dutch Prime Minister Colijn to Form an Extraordinary Cabinet; London Exchange Rate Shows Continued Rise in Guilder Value

Amsterdam Queen Wilhelmina has instructed former Prime Minister Colijn to form a new cabinet. According to general opinion here, Colijn will soon ask all factions to support his plan to form an extraordinary cabinet, but this plan must be approved by Parliament. (National Telegraph, 28th)

Amsterdam The news that Colijn was summoned to form a cabinet caused the guilder's value to continue to rise. It is expected that Colijn will form a new cabinet this afternoon or at the latest tomorrow. (Reuters, 29th)

(London) The news that Queen Wilhelmina of the Netherlands ordered former Prime Minister Colijn to reorganize the government has greatly changed the trend in the foreign exchange market today. Speculators have rushed to cover their positions, scrambling to buy Dutch guilders previously sold by the Dutch, which has caused the guilder's value to rise from 7.365 to 7.31. The discount rate for three-month futures has fallen from 34 to 26. Although the hope that the Dutch guilder will adhere to the gold standard is greatly increased, well-informed sources claim that the Dutch Bank has lost £20 million worth of gold, so its defense capabilities have been weakened. People feel that if Colijn can form a new government, it will be more difficult for him to handle matters than before the economic bill was proposed. The previous government headed by Colijn collapsed because of this bill. (Reuters, 29th)

US Gold and Silver Statistics: Last Year's Silver Imports Were Extremely High

(Washington) The US Department of Commerce's international balance of payments report states that last year's silver exports remained very small, totaling only US$16,551,000, but the amount of silver imported was extremely large, totaling US$102,725,000. The report also stated that from July 19 of last year to March 29 of this year, the US Treasury obtained a total of US$395,000,000 in silver. In addition to silver, the inflow of gold was even greater. Calculated at US$35 per ounce, the imported gold was worth a total of US$1,187,000,000. In addition, last year's surplus in US foreign trade was US$478,000,000, the largest amount since 1930. (National Telegraph, 28th)

(Washington) According to recent statistics, the value of gold imported from the Philippines to the United States in the first half of this year was US$6.6 million, more than the US$5.84 million in the same period last year, an increase of more than US$700,000. The value of silver flowing into the United States in the first half of this year was US$94,000, more than the US$40,000 in the same period last year, which proves that the production of the mining industry and agricultural production on the Philippine Islands is indeed great. Previously, some people thought that once the Philippine Islands became independent, they would have no way to survive economically. This point can be understood immediately. (National News Agency, 28th)

Hurricane to Strike Taiwan and Advance Towards Fujian

Taipei The hurricane moving straight towards Taiwan from the South Pacific was still 400 kilometers east of Keelung on the morning of the 29th. It is expected to strike the entire island of Taiwan late on the 29th. The military is on standby alert. (Japanese United News, 29th)

(Tokyo) Central Meteorological Observatory technician Arakawa said that the hurricane with a speed of 20 meters per second passed Ishigaki Island in Okinawa Prefecture on the 28th and blew westward. From the evening of the 29th to the morning of the 30th, southern Taiwan will be severely hit by it. This hurricane is still in the process of development, so it will increase its speed to 30 meters per second when it reaches Taiwan. Although its center will pass through the south, the entire island will inevitably suffer great damage. After passing through Taiwan, it will advance towards Fujian Province in China. The Japanese mainland can avoid its harm. (Japanese United News, 29th)

Hurricane Returns to Fuzhou

(Fuzhou) Fuzhou saw another hurricane on the 29th, with strong force. According to a telegram from Taipei, a new and stronger hurricane will arrive here on the 30th. Currently, all ships on the Min River have suspended navigation and entered the port to prevent damage. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Xiamen) Due to storms and rain on the 23rd and 24th, there was severe flooding in Zhangzhou and Quanzhou, and the damage to the Zhangzhou-Quanzhou-Fuzhou Highway was extremely heavy. According to the Provincial Automobile Management Office, 50,000 zhang (a Chinese unit of length, approximately 3.3 meters) of the road were damaged. The Construction Department is designing repairs. Cars will be able to travel directly to Quanzhou and Xiamen on the 29th. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Nanjing) The Central Meteorological Observatory reported that the hurricane reached the island of Taiwan in the afternoon of the 29th, and is now moving westward with extremely strong winds. It will land between Wenzhou and Xiamen. There are strong winds and rain in Guangdong and Fujian. There are showers along the coast of Zhejiang. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River have been affected. The highest temperature in Nanjing on the 29th was only 96 degrees. (Central News Agency, 29th)

Two Foreigners Kidnapped by Bandits in Inner Mongolia

(Beiping) News received here today, two foreigners, one being Mr. Jones, former secretary of Lloyd George, and currently a Far East traveler for the Manchester Guardian, and one being Dr. Mueller, a representative of a British company stationed in the military, were both kidnapped by bandits while traveling by car from Zhangjiakou to Dolon Nor. A ransom of 100,000 yuan is demanded. The Russian driver was also kidnapped at the time, but was later released and will return to Zhangjiakou tomorrow, probably carrying a letter from the bandits. Mr. Jones has been in China for several weeks, recently traveling in Inner Mongolia. To get to Dolon Nor from Zhangjiakou, he must pass through Juye, a large part of which is not stationed by troops, as they were withdrawn at the request of the Japanese. Dr. Mueller speaks fluent Chinese. The kidnapping took place near Baochang, 83 miles northeast of Zhangjiakou, not far from Guyuan. (Reuters, 29th)

(Beiping) Briton Jones and German Dr. Mueller, after leaving Prince De, the leader of Inner Mongolia, in Pangjiang Ula, were kidnapped by bandits on Saturday while traveling from Dolon Nor to Zhangjiakou. The two left Dolon Nor on Friday by long-distance bus. The bandits were disbanded soldiers who first shot at the car, hitting the engine twice, and then searched the car for valuables. Jones, Dr. Mueller, the Russian driver, and a Chinese servant were all taken to the mountains near Baochang, around noon on Saturday. At 6 p.m. that night, the driver and the Chinese servant escaped to Baochang and reported to the local officials. The British authorities here have notified the Chinese authorities of Jones' kidnapping, asking them to pay attention and rescue him as soon as possible. They have also telegraphed the authorities in Zhangjiakou, asking them to intercept Captain Scott, the Deputy Military Attaché of the British Embassy, who is currently traveling in Inner Mongolia and returning to that place. It is heard that Scott will be ordered to stay in Zhangjiakou to investigate this case and find a way to rescue the two. It is also heard that the Japanese military authorities have expressed their willingness to assist Chinese personnel in rescuing the two kidnapped men. Currently, 500 Chinese military police have entered the mountains to pursue the bandits. (Reuters, 29th)

(Beiping) It is now known that the two foreigners who were kidnapped by bandits near Guyuan are Jones, former secretary of British Prime Minister Lloyd George, now a Far East reporter for the Manchester Guardian, and Dr. Mueller, a representative of the German news agency. (Reuters, 29th)

Dolon Becomes the Economic Center of Eastern Chahar

(Beiping) Dolon is the central area connecting Jehol, Chahar, Inner and Outer Mongolia. After the Eastern Chahar issue was resolved, many Japanese people went to the area for inspection and trade. The South Manchuria Railway Company also started holding a Japanese commodity sample market in Dolon on the 20th of this month. The Mongolian people also held the Dolon Lama Temple Fair. Therefore, Dolon has a tendency to become the economic center of Eastern Chahar. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

Tianjin River Affairs Bureau Orders Attention to Dikes

(Tianjin) The water level of the Yongding River at the Huilongmiao station was 9 feet on the 29th, with no major fluctuations. On the evening of the 28th, the river water was full of floating grass and was turbid in color. The River Bureau determined that it was raining upstream and the water will rise sharply within days. They have ordered all sections of employees to prepare to go to the dikes for protection. Also, the water flow at the Lugou Bridge is very rapid, and the scouring force is very strong. The southern dike of the siltation area in the middle of the downstream is also mostly scoured and destroyed. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Beiping) The Douhe, Yunmei River, and Huanxiang River are experiencing flash floods, and several thousand acres of farmland on both sides have been flooded. The autumn harvest is hopeless. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

Yangtze River Water Level Report

(Nanjing) The Yangtze River Conservancy Commission received water level reports from various places on the 29th. Except for Chongqing rising 6 fen (a Chinese unit of length, approximately 3.3 mm), Wanxian rising 1.2 cun (a Chinese unit of length, approximately 3.3 cm), Nanjing rising 3 fen, and Zhenjiang rising 9 fen, all other places have receded. (Central Telegram, 29th)

(Nanjing) On the 29th, the water level at Xiaguan, according to the Public Works Bureau's records, was a maximum of 6.823 meters and a minimum of 6.678 meters, an increase of 0.023 meters compared to the 28th. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

Economic Commission Studies and Implements the "Returning Fields to Lakes" Method

(Nanjing) The Economic Commission is studying implementation methods for returning cultivated land to lakes in order to reduce flooding. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek proposed this after the major flood of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), and two principles were decided, as well as an implementation method. Over the years, due to many national affairs, it has not been implemented. Now the Economic Commission has brought up the old matter again, and will conduct practical research on how to implement the above method. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

(Nanjing) During the flood in the 20th year of the Republic (1931), Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who was also the President of the Executive Yuan at the time, proposed the "Returning Fields to Lakes" plan at the State Council meeting. The Economic Commission believes that this year's flood is once again serious, and is currently studying the implementation method for returning cultivated land to lakes. According to the proposal, it was resolved at the time to assign the ministers of the Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Industry, and Ministry of Communications to convene specialized personnel and relevant agencies for consultation. Later, two principles were decided: 1. River fields and beaches that obstruct the normal flow of water and lake fields that encroach on the normal flood storage capacity should be abolished. 2. River fields, lake fields, and beaches, except for those that should be abolished according to the above regulations, will still be reserved. In addition, five implementation methods were also decided. However, due to many national affairs, it has not been implemented. This time, the Economic Commission has brought up the old matter again and will conduct practical research on the implementation method. (Central News Agency, 29th)

(Nanjing) Han Fuju telegraphed the Economic Commission, requesting that they quickly plan methods to dredge and manage the Yellow River to alleviate the flooding. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

It has also been decided to add civil and criminal courts to hear backlog cases. (Special Dispatch, 29th)

Remnants of Liu Guitang's Bandits Invade Xinglong County

(Beiping) On the 26th, more than 700 remnants of Liu Guitang's bandits suddenly invaded Yongan Bao, Xinglong County. They had over 500 rifles and two machine guns, and they extorted and robbed residents, and kidnapped people for ransom. The local militia, consisting of 85 men, launched an attack on the night of the 27th, leading to a fierce battle. After about twelve hours of fighting, the militia, being outnumbered and running out of ammunition and reinforcements, were disarmed by the bandits. Sino-British Nanjing Incident: Remaining Payment Determined

(Nanjing) The Sino-British Nanjing Incident occurred in 1927. The Sino-British governments reached a mutual understanding and peacefully resolved it early on. However, due to a dispute over the conversion of the indemnity paid by China to Britain, the British side expressed dissent, and it has not been completely resolved. Now, after repeated consultations between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the British Ambassador, Sir Knatchbull-Hugessen, China will make a final payment of 199,700+ national currency. The Sino-British Nanjing Incident is thus completely resolved. (Special dispatch, 29th)

Public Telegram

A telegram from the Shimen County of Hunan Province appeals to the National Government Executive Yuan Relief Committee, the China International Famine Relief Commission, all organizations, all charities, all newspapers, and all groups: Shimen County is located in a remote area of western Hunan, with obstructed transportation. Natural disasters and banditry have occurred one after another, and the people have long suffered. Last year, a severe drought plagued the area, and the county's harvest was less than 20 percent of normal. The disaster situation was already serious. Unexpectedly, heaven did not tire of inflicting misfortune. Now, during the time when the autumn crops should be flourishing, we have suddenly suffered an unprecedented flood. Shimen County has the Ying River running through it. The upper reaches consist of many chaotic mountains, and the river flows swiftly and turbulently, making it extremely dangerous. Between summer and autumn, mountain waters erupt, and the situation is even more dire. Therefore, the slightest spring rain turns into a massive disaster, but even then, it usually only affects one or a few places, making it easier to remedy. Even in 1931, although boats could sail on the foot of the mountains in the county seat, it was not as severe as this time. Unexpectedly, from July 3rd to 6th this year, continuous rain fell, and mountain torrents erupted. All the large and small villages and important towns along the 200+ li of the Ying River were swept away by the raging waves. Farmland turned into gravel, houses were destroyed, and the topography changed. People who were caught off guard were drowned. Those who managed to escape were left with nothing. At this time, the autumn harvest is hopeless, and it is even harder to care about spring farming. The remaining survivors are destitute and lack both food and clothing. Suicides by drowning are reported daily, and corpses are everywhere. The stench of decay is overwhelming, and epidemics are raging, with no medical care available. Those who do not die from fire will die from disease. Alas, what a terrible fate for our people! We, who are concerned about our homeland and feel the pain deeply, have organized the Flood Relief Association of Fellow Townsmen Abroad. We are appealing to all parties, hoping to extend the life of the dying disaster victims for one more day. We have long admired your organizations' compassionate hearts and concern for suffering. Hearing of this catastrophe, you must feel deeply saddened. We respectfully request that you quickly grant us a large sum of money to provide generous relief, so that we can receive timely aid and save many lives. We are awaiting your orders in anticipation. Sincerely, the Flood Relief Association of Fellow Townsmen Abroad from Shimen County, Hunan Province.

Shandong Province, Dongping: Three More Breaches in the Canal; Floodwaters Threaten to Enter Dong'e Lake

Correspondent from Jinan: Amidst the reports of the Yellow River overflowing in western Shandong, the canal in Dongping County burst through three breaches west of Anshan Town on the evening of the 27th due to the Yellow River filling it. The water was extremely strong, and nearby villages were completely submerged. The terrain here is higher in the southwest than in the northwest, which may cause the water to combine with nearby slope water and flow directly into Dong'e Lake. The Xin Dian breach downstream of the Jinning Canal has already flowed to the Wujiawan northeast of the Si River. Its northward flow has reached the Jinpu Railway. Fortunately, precautions were taken early. Soldiers and civilians blocked the culverts and built crescent-shaped levees, so the water did not flood. The Nanyang and Shushan Lakes are still rising due to the inflow of the Yellow River water from Jiaxiang and Shanxian and the breaches of the Yun and Wen rivers. Fortunately, the dikes along the lake are in good condition, and Jinning and the northern part of the province may be spared from disaster. The waters of Nanyang Lake have reached the highway foundation north of Nandazibo, and are connected to the Yellow River water, reaching a width of 27 li. As for the plan to cut reeds in Nanyang Lake to facilitate drainage, the Jinning County Magistrate Zhen Guangyuan led the teachers, staff, and students of the rural schools in Qiaoshiqiao, Wang Guitun, and other three locations on the 27th, along with Commander Liu and Battalion Commander Wang of the 58th Brigade of the 20th Division with a battalion of soldiers on 100 boats. They departed. The work area extended from the north bank of the canal and between the Zhao and Wang Rivers, starting with direct cutting to Nanyang Town, about 60 li long. It will take about one week to complete. The Yellow River water in Heze has recently receded by 4 inches. The Yellow River water inside the Zhukou dike has retreated, revealing flat ground, and gradually stabilizing. On the 26th, heavy winds and rain hit Yutai, and the dikes along the coast of Nanyang Lake became dangerous works. People are working hard to protect them.

Jiangxi Province Has a Good Early Rice Harvest, But Disaster Areas Have Nothing

Correspondent from Nanchang: Jiangxi is an important agricultural area of the Yangtze River. The harvest of three seasons of rice, early, middle, and late, is about 130 million dan per year. Since the beginning of spring this year, there has been sufficient rain. The early rice grew well. However, due to continuous rains at the turn of June and July, the water in the Gong River rose sharply. The rivers, lakes, and the Yangtze River in Northeast Jiangxi: Xiushui, Raohe, Xinhe, Ganjiang, Poyang Lake, all overflowed. Many people along the rivers and lakes collapsed. The low-lying areas are still one color of water. All crops are gone. Disaster victims are scattered and fleeing. However, in areas outside of the permanent disaster zones in the province, the early rice harvest in the mountainous areas and higher elevations is good. The early rice in southwest Jiangxi and the Fu River basin in eastern Jiangxi is more than 80% good. As the new grain enters the market, rice prices are falling in various places. The price of rice in this city, which was formerly 11 yuan per stone, has now fallen below 10 yuan, and is still falling.

Suzhou: Embezzlement Case Involving Farmland Tax - Bankruptcy Compensation

He submitted this to the county government for approval yesterday. However, the county government learned that Zhu also owned three self-built houses at the west entrance of the alley, and that these houses should also be sold together to cover the compensation. As for the criminal matter, whether to send it to the judiciary will be decided by the county government after reporting to the civil and financial departments and the provincial government.

Provincial Committee Randomly Checks and Re-examines Smokers

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee recently dispatched Lv Xingfu, a member of the committee, to various counties to conduct on the spot checks and re-examinations of smokers in order to assess the effectiveness of the anti-smoking efforts in each county. The provincial capital designated more than ten names per county from the list of smokers who had quit smoking, and instructed Member Lv to randomly check them upon arrival. Now, Lv has come to Wuxi yesterday to inspect the County Anti-Smoking Association and the Smoking Cessation Center, and to conduct random checks and re-examinations of smokers. It is said that the provincial capital has prescribed two methods for re-examining smokers in order to prevent relapses: one is to have the county association submit a certain number of people on a regular basis, which the province will circle and designate for re-examination; the other is to have the province randomly select a certain number of people from the smokers' registry of each county and send staff or order the county to handle the re-examination.

Huangnianqiao Town: Bandits Rob and Injure Police

At the Zhao Mao General Merchandise Store in Huangnianqiao Town, about 11 li from Erling Town, more than a dozen bandits suddenly appeared the night before, wearing short black clothes, carrying long and short guns and iron rods, and broke into the store. The store owner, Wang Hechu, was awakened from his dream and, unable to escape, was grabbed by the bandits and forced to reveal the location of the hidden money. When Wang refused, he was beaten and injured. The bandits then rummaged through the boxes and cabinets, looting everything, and left after about half an hour. Upon hearing the report, the Erling 6th Sub-Station immediately ordered police officers to pursue and capture them. The bandits had already fled, so they telegraphed the Danyang General Bureau and requested that police be sent to Erling to assist in the capture. Upon receiving the telegram, the General Bureau immediately ordered Inspector Peng and Police Officer Guo to lead the police out of the city and search along the highway towards Ke. When they reached the first wooden bridge about 5 li from the city, two barefoot men wearing blue short shirts and trousers suddenly approached. Seeing their panicked expressions, they immediately found many stolen goods on the spot and detained them. Inspector Peng then led the police officers to continue searching forward. After another half a li, they saw five more people approaching and ordered them to stop, intending to search them. Unexpectedly, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. With a loud bang, Police Officer Zhu Hongtong was shot and killed. The police officers immediately returned fire. The gunfire was intense for a while. As a result, two bandits were killed, and two were captured. One rifle was seized. The remaining three bandits escaped. It was not until dawn that the body of the deceased police officer Zhu Hongzhang and the two captured bandits were brought into the city. The bodies of the two dead bandits were temporarily placed under the Yin Gong Bridge outside Dongdou. According to the two bandits in the bureau, one named Gao Sheng and the other named Wang Guofa, they confessed to the robbery in Huangnianqiao without denial. They have now been sent to the county for interrogation.

Jiashan: Teasing a Dwarf Child Leads to a Fatal Incident

Huang Gengxiang, originally from Tiantai, runs a bakery in Gan Yao Town in this county, and his business is doing well. He has a domestic servant surnamed Zhang, who is only 14 years old, with a small body and very naughty nature, which Huang dislikes. The day before yesterday, Huang ordered the dwarf child to carry a cake tray and sell along the road. At the end of the market, he fell asleep on the grass. Unexpectedly, someone secretly moved and hid the cake tray. When the child woke up, the cake tray was gone. Extremely frightened and wanting to cry, he was afraid of being beaten by Huang and hurried back. He questioned everyone in the store, and while they were arguing, Huang heard them. He grabbed the dwarf child, beat him severely, and ordered his wife to send the child back to his hometown. Thereupon, the aunt and nephew took a boat to Shan. After landing, they were still far from the station, so they walked west along the railway track. Just as they reached the Gou Shou Jingyang Bridge, a train came speeding from behind. In a hurry to get out of the way, both of them accidentally fell into the river. Passersby went into the water to rescue them. Huang's wife was fortunately unharmed, but the dwarf child was drowned. His body has not been found yet.

Local News

Shanghai Newspaper Association's Talk on the Amendment of the Publication Law

After the amendment of the Publication Law was passed by the Legislative Yuan, newspaper industries in various places rose up to discuss it. They considered that the amendment to the law imposed strict restrictions on the news industry and telegraphed the authorities one after another, requesting reconsideration. In the past two days, newspapers reported that Legislator Chuan Bingchang and Vice President of the Judicial Yuan Qin Zhen made statements, saying that after the promulgation of the amended Publication Law, if there were any obstacles that were difficult to implement, they should be carefully revised. The reporter interviewed the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Newspaper Association yesterday and inquired about this matter. According to the spokesperson of the association, in order to seek legitimate freedom for the press, the association believes that the Publication Law has many restrictions and that the points that should be noted have been telegraphed to the Central Political Council, requesting that it be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for reconsideration. This procedure, as Legislator Fu Bingchang said, if the Central Political Council submits it for reconsideration, it can be discussed again. Otherwise, the Legislative Yuan has no power to change the law that has been passed. It can be seen that although a bill has been passed by the Legislative Yuan, if it is believed that it is still necessary to study and revise it, it can be remedied by following the reconsideration procedure. If we wait until it is promulgated and implemented and then encounter difficulties before seeking revision, it seems that we will spend too much time. As for publishing personal or family privacy, it belongs to private legal interests. Therefore, the criminal law on defamation requires prosecution. The provisions of Articles 309 to 313 of the Criminal Law are very detailed and are not without restrictions. If the provisions of the amended Publication Law are followed, the competent authorities have the right to prosecute, which is in obvious conflict with the principles of criminal law.

Kong Xiangxi, He Yingqin, etc. Took the Same Train to Beijing Last Night

Kong Xiangxi, Acting President of the Executive Yuan, came to Shanghai a few days ago to handle the business of the Central Bank. It is difficult to predict whether they will return to Shanghai.

The Hurricane Is Still Far From Shanghai; It Is Difficult to Predict Whether It Will Hit Shanghai

The Shanghai Evening Post reported that the barometer is falling today (29th) and the weather changes are uncertain, making the future weather difficult to predict. An extremely strong hurricane is currently attacking the coast of China from due east of Taiwan. This hurricane is developing very strongly and progressed quite quickly at the end of last week, but it is still far from Shanghai today and has not yet had a direct impact on Shanghai. Judging from its current direction westward or west-northwest, its severe power can be felt within days. If it deviates towards Shanghai, it will be even more severe. Its current position is greatly hindering southern shipping. The mail plane to Guangzhou tomorrow may not be able to pass safely. If the direction of the hurricane does not change, it will land near Fuzhou and disappear in Fujian Province. However, there is concern that it may change direction, in which case Shanghai will at least be on the edge of the affected area.

Ministry of Finance Unifies the Currency System; Collects and Melts Miscellaneous Currencies to Mint Decimal Subsidiary Coins

According to the Central News Agency, China's currency system has always been very chaotic, which has greatly affected the livelihood of ordinary people. The authorities of the Ministry of Finance believe that it is necessary to unify it immediately, so the Currency System Research Committee of the Ministry of Finance was established. The committee also established a Shanghai office to assist in the affairs of the committee. Since its establishment, the committee has been actively conducting research on the national currency system, sparing no effort. According to reporters' inquiries in the financial sector, the unification of the national currency system is very difficult. This is a major matter, and it is necessary to conduct detailed research beforehand before proceeding step by step. Otherwise, the disadvantages will be seen before the advantages are achieved. The chaotic state of currency in various provinces and cities in China cannot be fully described in a few words, and the provinces of Sichuan, Guangdong, and Fujian are the worst. The more complex the domestic currency, the more exploitation there is in the exchange, and the small businessmen are the ones who suffer the most. Before proceeding with the unification, we should first investigate the chaotic state of currency in various places across the country, and then mint decimal currency to replace it. The collection and melting of miscellaneous currencies in various places will not be effective in a short period of time. Therefore, on the one hand, the Ministry of Finance has the Central Mint minting new coins every day and circulating them on the market. On the other hand, the Central Bank is collecting and melting miscellaneous currencies in various places. As for the use of decimal currency to mint subsidiary coins with nickel and other materials, it is said that the Currency System Research Committee of the Ministry of Finance is actively planning it.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Si Hai Ship Begins Selling Hong Kong Tickets; Chinese Ship Owners Will Start Implementation From the Hai Li Ship Starting August 3rd

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has been selling Hong Kong passenger tickets and has been negotiating with the Hong Kong government many times. Since July, the Hong Kong authorities have recognized China as a country that has signed the Nine-Nation Maritime Safety Convention and allowed it to issue passenger licenses, but each ship must first obtain the international navigation safety certificate issued by the ministry. The Hong Kong government can then issue passenger licenses based on this safety certificate. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has sent Zhou Houkun, deputy director of the ship department, to Beijing to collect the international navigation safety certificate from the Ministry of Transportation. They will be distributed to the shipowners of the Haiyuan, Haining, Haili, and Haizhen to be handed over to the Hong Kong government for verification when they arrive in Hong Kong. Then, the passenger licenses will be issued to each ship. Now, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has received instructions from the Ministry of Transportation that the Hong Kong authorities have publicly recognized our country as one of the countries of the Nine-Nation Maritime Safety Convention, and the international navigation safety certificate has been issued. Passenger tickets to Hong Kong can now be sold to benefit passengers. The bureau has also obtained the Hong Kong passenger license and allowed the passenger stock to sell Hong Kong tickets for all classes on the Si Hai ship from today. The Haiyuan ship will depart tomorrow. This ship could have sold Hong Kong passenger tickets (because the shipowners are Westerners), and the first Chinese-owned ship to sell Hong Kong tickets is the Haili ship that will leave Shanghai on August 3rd. The current ticket prices are: First class (Deluxe Cabin) - 50 yuan, First class cabin - 24 yuan, Second class cabin - 17 yuan, Third class - 9.5 yuan, Fourth class - 7.6 yuan.

The Industry and Commerce Revival Association Held Its First Reception for Owners Yesterday; Chairman Wang Yansong Gave the Opening Speech; Application Forms and Industrial Survey Forms Were Issued on the Spot

The Industry and Commerce Revival Committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce held its first reception for factory owners and representatives at the chamber at 9 a.m. yesterday. Chairman Wang Yansong gave the opening speech and issued small business credit loan application forms and industrial survey forms of the committee. The details are recorded as follows:

Distribution of Forms

The first reception for factory owners and representatives was attended by more than 100 companies, including Kai Cheng Acid Factory, Da Zhong Dye Factory, China Porcelain Factory, East Asia Machine Factory, Zhongxing Crucible Factory, China Chemical Industry Company, Taishan Brick and Tile Factory, Tianzhang Paper Mill, Senji Paper Mill, Dongfang Nianhong Company, and Yili Soda Factory. More than 100 representatives, including Jin Baoting and Xu Wengui, attended. On this day, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce accepted the commission of the Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee and issued loan application forms for the first day. Wang Yansong, Chairman of the Revival Committee, gave the opening speech. Xi Yushu, Director of the Investigation Team, explained the importance of writing the industrial survey form. Lin Shaofeng, a representative of the Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee, also attended the meeting to explain the procedures for filling out the loan application form. At about 11 o'clock, the industrial survey form of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the application form for industrial and commercial loans were distributed on the spot, and the meeting was adjourned.

Opening Speech

Chairman Wang Yansong said in his opening speech: "Today is the first time that the association has invited the owners and representatives of various factories in this city. It coincides with the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce entrusting the Industry and Commerce Loan Committee to issue loan application forms, which also starts today. Therefore, the number of people attending the meeting is more than expected, and the reception is not very thoughtful. I am very sorry. As for the significance of the association inviting the owners and representatives of various factories, it has been described in the official letter. The association is an organization organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce based on the motion of the Sixth Member Congress. Its task is to work with the industrial and commercial circles to raise appropriate plans in order to seek effective relief. This task is extremely important, and it is not something that the colleagues of the association can bear with their thoughts and talents. However, in the face of national difficulties, we dare not avoid difficulties and shirk our responsibilities, so as to avoid inevitable accusations. This requires joint efforts and cannot but be based on the principle that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country, and we hope that the industrial and commercial circles will enthusiastically advance and cooperate sincerely to reduce the inevitable accusations. In our country's society, we are always happy to criticize various problems, but the result of the criticism often makes the work of solving the problem unable to increase benefits. For example, the association is an organization that plans to relieve the unprecedented difficulties of industry and commerce. Critics often accuse it of being slow because it cannot immediately propose a proper plan after its establishment. This kind of criticism is extremely admirable, but it should not be overlooked that there are various difficulties, such as increasing tariffs and controlling foreign exchange, which are the best ways to curb imports and revive industry and commerce, but they cannot be implemented temporarily due to environmental reasons. Other things, such as flood attacks, are also external causes that promote the decline of industry and commerce. The best way to relieve the disaster is to dredge the river channel, but due to financial reasons, we can only do prevention. Therefore, the formulation of a plan must take into account both the actual strength and the environment. The so-called plan is not a paper article or an oral speech that embodies personal ideals, but a method of studying the factual environment, collecting thoughts from many parties, carefully sorting them out, and seeking to conform to the environmental facts to solve the problem. If the association, after its establishment, does not conduct practical research on the current environment and only proposes methods immediately based on one aspect of the problem's needs, I am afraid that this method will inevitably encounter the difficulty of being too hasty. Therefore, it is necessary to learn from the past and know the hidden things as a warning. The plan for governing a business is the same as the policy for governing a country. Therefore, the plan cannot be obtained in one case. If it is so easy, industry and commerce will never fall into decline and suffer the pain of calling for help without a door. Colleagues have recently invited leaders and experts from various industries to discuss the reasons for the decline of industry and commerce. They feel that the reason is that there is no appropriate plan for governing the industry. The so-called no appropriate plan for governing the industry means that there is no sound organization in terms of economy and personnel, and there are no accurate statistics on production and consumption. Without statistics, there is no way to know oneself, and without organization, there is no way to know others. If you don't know others and yourself, you will certainly not be able to cope with the attacks of commercial warfare, and gradual decline is inevitable. If we want to revive industry and commerce, we must attach importance to investigation, statistics, and training in order to formulate plans and promote the application of plans. Therefore, the association's work starts with investigation. The obtained investigation materials are analyzed by statistical methods to analyze the reasons for the decline of industry and commerce. Experts are invited to study and predetermine a reasonable plan. On the other hand, we can pay more attention to training so that managers and staff know how to be loyal and dutiful in order to seek the soundness of their own abilities, and then submit them to the government for practical assistance. In this case, it is not necessarily hopeless to save industry and commerce that is trapped in the phenomenon of recession. Today, the general opinion is that the only way to relieve industry and commerce is to increase chips. This is undoubtedly true, but how can we make the ideal of increasing chips a reality? We must study it. For example, doctors all know that a certain prescription can cure the disease, but they also know the place to buy the medicine and the way to reach the place to buy the medicine before prescribing the medicine. Otherwise, even if there is a good prescription, what is the use of the disease? Now, to take a step back, assuming that the proposal to increase chips will become a reality tomorrow, and we ask the critics to distribute it on our behalf, I am afraid that the critics will also need investigation and statistical materials and are unwilling to distribute it without selection. It can be seen that investigation and statistics must be valued in the future. The association has already started working on the work that must be valued in the future today, so it should not be described as slow. Therefore, if we want to save the declining industry and commerce, we must first invigorate ourselves and develop the spirit of self-help, and then we can expect people to rescue us, and we can also advance to rescue others. The association's investigation, statistics, and training work are based on the source of the disease and strive for self-invigoration and self-help methods, which can complement the proposal to increase chips. I hope that the enthusiasts and pioneers in the industrial sector can provide sincere cooperation and assistance to the association's work. What I want to solemnly state on behalf of my colleagues today is that first, the association will absolutely keep all kinds of investigation materials confidential and will not leak them except for the research of the staff. If there are certain materials that are more important to keep confidential, you can also submit them to the association's executive director in writing to be kept more strictly. Second, the association's current work is limited to the 43 industries that have been determined, but the association is also willing to sincerely welcome other industries outside the scope of the 43 industries who are willing to cooperate with the association according to the initial working procedures.

Investigation Instructions

Yesterday was the first day that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce forwarded the application forms for small loans for industrial and commercial credit. It is estimated that there are more than 400 national goods factories and shops, and about 400 forms have been issued. It is stipulated that the period for issuing forms is from 9:00 am to 5:00 pm every day, except for holidays. In addition, the instructions for the association's industrial survey form state, "The purpose of the association's investigation is to find out the reasons for the decline of industry and commerce. It is necessary to have a clear understanding of the current phenomenon of each industrial and commercial organization before seeking relief, and then there will be a path to follow. For this reason, the filling of the investigation form must sweep away the common state of concealing the disease and avoid medical treatment. Based on the facts, talk about the source of the disease, so that effective cooperation and assistance can be expected. The forms issued by the association are for research purposes only and are kept confidential from the outside world. It is especially hoped that the various items listed will be filled in in detail, and please attach your opinions on relief." "Regarding the statement of opinions on relief, it must be divided into two categories: opinions on relief for oneself should be listed as the first category, and opinions on relief for the industry in general should be listed as the second category. Regarding the opinions on relief for oneself, it is best to list in detail the production efficiency and restoration guarantee that can be increased after obtaining relief. If the writing space in the original form is not enough, you can write on a separate sheet."

The China National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association Hosted the Press Last Night

The China National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association hosted a banquet for reporters from various newspapers at the Deng Tuomo Hotel on Ningbo Road last night. Reporters from Shen Bao, Xin Bao, and other newspapers attended and were warmly received by the standing committee members of the association. The banquet began at 7:30 PM. Mr. Yuan Ludeng of the association stood up first and expressed his gratitude to the reporters for their presence and spoke of the necessity to maintain the national cigarette industry, relying on the guidance and assistance of the press for promotion. Subsequently, Mr. Shen Weiting and Mr. Wang Xiaolai of the association delivered sincere speeches. Finally, Mr. Yan Duhe was elected by the reporters to give a reply. Toasts were raised repeatedly, and the guests and hosts parted joyfully at around 10:00 PM. The details of the gathering are recorded below.

List of Guests: Reporters from various newspapers included Ma Chonggan, Zhao Junhao, Jin Huating, Huang Jiping, Hu Zhongchi (all from Shen Bao), Li Haoran, Yan Duhe, Quan Kongwo, Jiang Xiyi (all from Xinwen Bao), Teng Shugu, Zong Dao (both from Shibao), He Xiya, Wu Han, Yang Yucheng (all from Chen Bao), Huang Tianpeng, Nie Shiqi (both from Shishi Xinbao), Qian Cangshuo, Wu Zhongyi (both from Min Bao), Zhang Ruogu, Cui Wanqiu, Zhu Chaoran (all from Da Wan Bao), Li Wu (from Zhonghua Ribao).

List of Hosts: Those responsible for hosting from the association included Yuan Ludeng, Wang Xiaolai, Shen Weiting, Bao Gengsheng, Ding Zhenbo, Shen Xuewen, Shen Xingde, Wang Junzhi, Ding Houqing, Wu Linzhi, Jing Yimeng, Sun Daosheng, and committee members Wu Peiyin and Gong Weiguan.

Speech by Shen Weiting: Tonight, our association has prepared this humble feast to entertain reporters from various newspapers. We are deeply honored that you have not hesitated to brave the summer heat to grace us with your presence and offer your guidance. I would now like to briefly present the purpose of maintaining national cigarettes for your consideration. Although cigarettes are a consumable item, their need is quite widespread in general social circumstances. Therefore, they are also popular in European and American countries. England and the United States are also famous tobacco-producing regions. The number of cigarettes and tobacco leaves exported each year is very large, accounting for an important position in foreign trade. Therefore, the government promotes and encourages it to help promote the development of the rural economy. As for the tobacco producing areas in our country, there are many. Their situation is similar to that of England and the United States. However, tobacco farmers often stick to old ways and do not know how to improve, resulting in slightly inferior quality. Therefore, for the sake of revitalizing the rural economy, tobacco leaves should be improved, and national cigarettes should be maintained. In other words, maintaining national cigarettes is also to revive the rural economy. From the perspective of the business conditions of Chinese cigarette factories, they have gradually felt sluggish in the most recent past few years. Since February of this year, they have felt a sharp decline and things have gotten worse. Shutdowns are frequently heard, and those who are lucky enough to be at work are also in a precarious situation due to sluggish sales. The general downturn is imaginable. There are many reasons for its cause, but the price cuts and competitive sales of foreign goods are the biggest reason. Today, Chinese factories are in a difficult situation, and it is increasingly difficult to support them. If they do not rise up together and seek to save them, then great difficulties will be on the rise. If unfortunately all Chinese factories collapse, not only will the right to operate the cigarette business be lost, but also more than 100,000 workers will be unemployed, and tobacco farmers will also feel panicked. Looking to the future, I cannot help but feel terrified. This is another reason why national cigarettes urgently need to be maintained. However, the way to maintain them depends on the collective efforts of everyone, and publicity and promotion are especially important. Newspapers are a powerful tool for propaganda, surpassing even three thousand Mauser rifles. Moreover, Shanghai is the center of national public opinion, and the newspapers are popular throughout the country. A loud call can change the views and opinions of society. Now that national cigarettes are in a dangerous position, please, based on your enthusiasm for protecting industry and promoting national products, do your best to support us, promote widely, and hope to give us some guidance to correct our shortcomings, so that the business of national cigarettes can be developed and promoted. We will be very grateful.

Speech by Yuan Ludeng: Briefly speaking, I believe that the national cigarette industry has had a vigorous appearance since the May 30th Movement. At this time, when the global economic downturn is sweeping, there is bound to be a feeling of past and present. The capital side may still be able to endure the pain and wait for the opportunity, but the labor side may not be able to cope. Therefore, today's maintenance is really more for the sake of the workers in the cigarette factory.

Speech by Wang Xiaolai: Briefly speaking, starting to maintain the national cigarette industry today is like mending the fold after the sheep is lost. It is too late, and the dream of brilliance has become a memory. It is a pity to say. I have put in a lot of effort into this industry, and all colleagues know the details. I remembered my twenty-fourth birthday, just at the time of the Restoration and the removal of braids. I needed half a tin of cigarettes a day. On that day, I got rid of my cigarette addiction. But for fellow smokers, they must smoke national cigarettes, and they must maintain it.

Speech by Yan Duhe: Briefly speaking, I have listened to the great views of everyone just now and admire them very much. Mr. Xiaolai’s self-narration of his story of quitting cigarettes is especially enough to set an example. Not many people in the world can do what he says and does. Speaking of myself, I need cigarettes every day, and my smoking amount is several times that. I have resolved to quit smoking five or six times, but I have never succeeded. Judging others by myself, there are certainly many people who are similar to me, or who have never thought of quitting. Cigarettes are a social need. It is a fact that smoking national cigarettes can greatly benefit tobacco farmers, and cigarette merchants are secondary. As for the press to promote national industrial and commercial industries, it is its natural duty, and it is not unique to the national cigarette industry. The news industry cannot transcend the world, and it must prosper together with the prosperity of various national industries. Therefore, our press is very happy to do its duty to promote national cigarettes. On behalf of the press, I would like to toast the national cigarette industry and wish it a gradual transition from maintenance to prosperity.

Shanghai Cholera Prevention Temporary Office Notice No. 2

(1) Four weeks ago, this office issued Cholera Notice No. 1. To date, no true cholera cases have been found in Shanghai or elsewhere. Fecal samples from patients with gastroenteritis in Nanchang, Wuhu, Jiujiang, Hangzhou, Suzhou, Ningbo, and other places have been tested bacteriologically and found to be non-cholera.

(2) Suspected cholera cases continue to occur in Shantou and Xiamen. On July 6th, Shantou and Xiamen each had one death, but neither was confirmed as true cholera. So far this year, it can be said that there is no cholera year.

(3) On July 18th, Shanghai newspapers carried a news item stating that two true cholera patients had been found in the Chinese Isolation Hospital on Huade Road, and that both had been cured within a few hours. After investigation, it was found that the whole thing was fabricated.

(4) The major floods in the Yangtze and Yellow River basins have caused great disasters. As a result, some newspapers have speculated that cholera may break out, but this is completely unfounded. The term "cholera" refers to an infectious disease caused by true cholera bacteria (i.e., Koch's comma bacillus). Ordinary summer gastroenteritis should not be hastily called cholera. In the past, the misuse of this term has unnecessarily restricted our country's commercial transportation and caused our country to be regarded as a source of evil epidemics.

(5) The highest temperature this summer was 100.8 degrees Fahrenheit (July 14th) and 100.5 degrees Fahrenheit (July 15th). Last year's highest temperature was 104.4 degrees Fahrenheit (July 12th). However, the humidity has been very high this summer, averaging over 90 daily, while last year it was below 90 for several days.

(6) Isolation hospitals in various districts have been opened to prevent emergencies. However, there are no true cholera patients, and even common gastroenteritis cases are not numerous. For example, the Xizang Road Isolation Hospital has only used saline injections forty times so far. Although there have been a few cases of heatstroke deaths among Chinese and Westerners, heatstroke cases are not common.

(7) The health authorities continue to make efforts to prevent cholera and other summer diseases. It must be said that the intellectual class still has some misunderstandings about the fact that watermelons and flies spread disease. Therefore, although locally produced melons and fruits are inexpensive and beautiful, overly cautious people are often willing to pay two yuan for imported fruits, while buying local products costs only two jiao. Some people think that the roots of melons in polluted fields can absorb bacteria, which is an overestimation. Only cut melons and fruits that are sprinkled with sewage or contaminated by contaminated flies and hands pose a risk of spreading infectious diseases, and only flies containing bacteria are dangerous.

(8) The number of people vaccinated against cholera is as follows: Shanghai City (as of July 23rd) 209,108, French Concession (as of July 25th) 62,440, International Settlement (as of June 30th) 84,883, Health Department of the Two Roads Bureau (as of May 31st) 8,543, totaling 464,974 people.

July 29, 1935, Chairman Wu Liande.

City Chamber of Commerce Organizes Verification and Exchange of Stamp Tax Tickets, Opens for Business on August 1st, First Handles the Procedures for Assembling and Verifying

Regarding the exchange of old stamp tax tickets for new tickets, since the City Chamber of Commerce received the Ministry of Finance's announcement of the exchange method, it has now begun preparations. It has been decided that the collection and verification will begin on August 1st, and a verification and exchange of stamp tax tickets office will be organized on the first floor of the chamber. Staff have been assigned to handle it, as detailed below.

Chamber of Commerce Public Notice

The City Chamber of Commerce issued a public notice stating that the Ministry of Finance has formulated six articles on the method of exchanging old stamp tax tickets for new tickets, which have been published in the newspaper. According to Article 2 of the method, old tickets that were registered last year and have been returned to the accounts for storage in accordance with the regulations must still be collected by the Chamber of Commerce first, and the commissioners dispatched by the provincial bureau will conduct detailed verification and seal them in the Chamber of Commerce for monthly exchange for new stamp tax tickets in accordance with Article 1. The current first step is to re-collect the registered old tickets that have been returned, verify them, and seal them before they can be exchanged for new tickets. Therefore, this notice is for all accounts that registered old stamp tax tickets in this chamber last year. Please submit the registered old stamp tax tickets to the Old Ticket Verification Office of this chamber starting from August 1st to await verification and sealing by the provincial committee in preparation for exchanging them for new tickets. The office hours of this chamber are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day except holidays. This is hereby announced.

Assigned Staff

The Stamp Tax Ticket Verification and Exchange Office organized by the Chamber of Commerce will also begin operations on August 1st. The Standing Committee assigned the following staff yesterday: Zhang Yukun from the Commercial Affairs Department, Zhang Lishen from the Finance Department, Yang Baoru from the Exhibition Hall, and Zhu Qirong. They will first discuss the verification and exchange procedures today in order to proceed with the handling.

Various Charitable Organizations Receive Tragic Reports of Flood Disasters from Various Provinces

The Chinese and Foreign Relief Association: Since this month, we have received telegrams from the Yellow River and Yangtze River areas, reporting that either entire cities have been submerged or that the land has been a vast expanse of water, all urgently requiring rescue. These have been compiled and reported in previous newspapers. The association has recently received further reports from various disaster areas, which are excerpted below: (1) The Juye County Government of Shandong Province telegraphed: "Heaven has afflicted Juye, and disasters have occurred year after year. This time, the Yellow River breached its banks at Dongzhuang in Juancheng, and the torrents rushed down, covering the fields. On the same day, it entered from the northwest of the county, irrigating Kangji and Taiping to the north, and rushing through Longhe to the south, and crossing the Zhu River to the east, surrounding the county seat. All six regions of Tai Kang, the majority of the Great Righteousness Yushan regions, and other regions have been submerged. The water is eight or nine feet deep on flat ground. Sorghum, grains, and beans have all been submerged. Houses and stored grains have been washed away, and the number of people and livestock drowned is countless. The disaster area is 120 li long from east to west and 30 to 40 li wide from north to south, affecting over 800 villages and approximately 200,000 disaster victims. They are scattered everywhere, and their plight is unbearable to witness. In addition to the county's urgent relief efforts and the diversion and accommodation of victims, we urgently request the swift allocation of relief funds to save the remaining survivors." (2) Gao Xiangfu and others, disaster victims from Jining County, Shandong Province, telegraphed: "The Yellow River has breached its banks, and the floodwaters have flowed south, from Jining to Jincheng and then to Tengyi. The disaster area is over 200 li in both directions. Most of the villages in between have been engulfed, and no grains have been left in the large fields. Over 2 million disaster victims have suddenly lost their homes and are forced to sleep in the open and eat in the wind, making their plight unbearable. We respectfully plead on behalf of the people for swift relief." (3) The government of Duchang County, Jiangxi Province, telegraphed on behalf of the people: "Our county is located along Poyang Lake and is naturally low-lying. Unexpectedly, in the last ten days of last month, heavy rains came down like pouring water, causing mountain floods and a sharp rise in the lake level. The entire area is a vast expanse of water, becoming a swamp. Fields and houses have been submerged, and livestock and property have been washed away. This kind of catastrophe is unprecedented in decades. Most of the refugees are temporarily living in the mountains, eating in the wind and sleeping in the open, with their livelihoods cut off. They are suffering from heat and cold, and deaths are occurring one after another. Their plight is so tragic that Zheng Xia could not depict it. We are appealing for the dispatch of personnel to the county to distribute urgent relief and save the people." (4) The Water Disaster Relief Committee of Yuan'an County, Hubei Province, wrote: "The disaster area of this flood in our county is vast, extending from Naxiangcheng in the north to Dangyang in the south, covering over a hundred li. Cities and towns have been turned into swamps. Not only crops and livestock have been swept away, but also the elderly and young people have been swept away by the waves. There are corpses piled up in ditches everywhere. Disaster victims have no place to live and no food to eat. Their cries of hunger are everywhere, and they are eagerly waiting for food. We are begging for urgent relief." (5) The Wu Zhen Chamber of Commerce and various groups in Nanzhang County, Hubei Province, reported: "On July 3rd, there were five days and nights of continuous rain in our town, causing mountain floods that submerged the model towns of Wufeng and other towns, and the villages of Foshan and other townships. Some parts of Lingxi and other townships were also submerged. The area of over 50 li has become a swamp. Over 8,000 households have been engulfed, over 1,000 people have drowned, over 200 people have been crushed to death by collapsed houses, and tens of thousands of mu of fields have been submerged. The disaster situation is extremely serious, unprecedented. Disaster victims are on the roads, crying for food. We are begging for relief." (6) The Fifth District Temporary Disaster Relief Committee of Qianjiang County, Hubei Province, wrote: "On the 8th of this month, the embankment near Zhongxiang Shiergong breached, and the water rushed down, with Qianjiang County directly in its path. The water level was over two zhang high. The people were unable to escape, and their fields, houses, livestock, and people were all swept away by the waves. The number of people and livestock drowned is countless. It is estimated that there are over 10,000 households and 80,000 people in the entire district. No household is complete, and no family is whole. The dead are already gone, and the living are eating in the wind and drinking dew. It seems that those who do not die in the water will also die of hunger. We are making this appeal and pleading for relief."

The Chinese Jiesheng Society recently received a telegram from Peng Zhanyuan and Wang Chenge Yang Liu Zhao, representatives from Juancheng, Yuncheng, Juhe, and Heze counties in Shandong Province, stating: "The Shandong region, including Zhencheng, Heze, Yuncheng, and Juye counties, has suffered repeated Yellow River disasters, numbering seven times. This year is the most severe. On the 10th of this month, the Yellow River suddenly breached its banks at Dongzhuang on the east bank of Juancheng County, directly cutting through the county borders of Juancheng, Heze, Yuncheng, and Juye to the east. The roads it passed through were still the areas that had been affected by the previous six disasters. The torrents surged, as if galloping horses. In one day and night, hundreds of li were submerged. Hundreds of villages were lost, with depths exceeding a zhang in deeper areas and a chi in shallower areas. Houses were swept away, and countless people and livestock were drowned. Cries of woe are everywhere, and all the people have become subjects of the waves. Starvation and drowning are intertwined, and the survivors have no way to continue their lives. Life and death are permanently separated. Some have lost their white-haired parents and cannot care for their families. Some have abandoned their nursing children. Those who are fortunate enough to escape are crowded on the embankments. They have no place to live or eat. Those who are trapped and have not come out are sleeping in the open ruins of villages. They are in urgent need of rescue. In addition, continuous rain has worsened the situation, with torrential downpours occurring frequently. The god of wind is stubborn and frequently raises huge waves. They are exposed to rain and wind, and their figures are haggard. The situation is tragic and unbearable to witness. If relief is not provided quickly, the millions of disaster victims who have not yet died will soon fill the ditches. We beg you to open your benevolent hearts and join us in this good deed. Please quickly send funds and dispatch personnel to provide relief to save the survivors, etc." The association provided tens of thousands of yuan in relief during the Heze County flood two years ago. This year, too many counties have been submerged, and we urgently want to provide relief and rescue. We have not yet raised enough funds and have prepared 1,000 bottles of Jiesheng Dan to send to Heze County to urgently treat the sick. If we can raise a significant amount of relief funds, we will carefully arrange urgent relief to save the victims from this tragic disaster. Compassionate and virtuous people at home and abroad, please open your wallets and create blessings. Why not come?

Seventy-Third Batch of Overseas Chinese Expelled from Japan Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday, Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to Implement Relief Plan

The seventy-third batch of four overseas Chinese expelled from Japan arrived in Shanghai yesterday. The plan is scheduled to be implemented, and a reporter from the Industrial and Commercial News Agency has learned the details, which are detailed below.

More Overseas Chinese Arriving in Shanghai

The seventy-third batch of overseas Chinese expelled from Japan, Chen Shaoyu, Zhou Xianren (from Ruian, Zhejiang), Liu Tingzhai, and Chen Zhuoqing (from Qingtian, Zhejiang), arrived in Shanghai on the Tsukuba Maru of the Japan Post Steamship Company from Tokyo yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. The ship docked at the Osaka Wharf, and they disembarked and temporarily resided in the Lao Gongxin Hotel on the 16th Pier. Their situation is pitiful. It is reported that the overseas Chinese intend to request registration with the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau today so that they can cultivate land in the Qiaole Village.

Relief Plan Scheduled for Implementation

The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau, in view of the fact that the returning overseas Chinese have suffered unemployment, displacement, and extreme suffering, and in order to implement relief, previously joined forces with the Shanghai Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau to discuss relief measures. Director Jian of the bureau also drafted a relief plan for the overseas Chinese and went to Beijing to suggest it to the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, so that diplomatic and domestic affairs could be carried out in unison. At the same time, the diplomatic authorities will negotiate with various countries regarding anti-Chinese incidents. This plan is a matter of urgency for providing relief to the overseas Chinese and is expected to be implemented soon.

Shops on Two Roads in the French Concession Request Landlords to Voluntarily Reduce Rent; Sent Letters to Landlords Yesterday Explaining Difficult Circumstances

Shops along Caishi Road and Route Paul Beau in the French Concession, considering the market to be depressed and affected by road construction, making it difficult to maintain operations, have unanimously requested relief from the French authorities and rent reductions, as previously reported. It is now learned that the rent reduction delegation of the shopkeepers and residents of the two roads sent letters yesterday to the landlords in the area, including Ji Zhenyu Company, Wing On Real Estate Company, Ruiji Company, Chen Yueting, Junyi Industrial Company, Yuelai Company, Thiele & Co., Chen Sanlin, Yuanchang Company, Xu Linji, Qin Xijiu, Shunji Company, Ruizheng Company, Sino-French Bank, Continental Property Management, Xingji Company, Gan Yifeng, Banque de l'Indochine, Thiele Company, Gu Lanji, Rixin Sheng, Xieji Company, Junji Company, Hanzhuang Jiyi Public Association, Jiyi Real Estate Company, Hengji Company, Tian Hongsheng, Lawyer Xu Shihao, Lin Shuangquan, China Industrial Bank, Rendao Company, and more than thirty other landlords, requesting them to voluntarily implement rent reductions. The original letter is recorded below: Respected Sirs, In recent years, Shanghai has been hit by the global economic downturn and the impact of rural bankruptcy in the interior, resulting in a depressed market that worsens daily and an extremely difficult social economy. As a result, finance is stagnant and shops are closing one after another. Shanghai, once known as the most prosperous city in the country, has turned into a desolate ancient ruin. Those who are operating shops in Shanghai today, in order to save the critical situation, have to lower their prices to attract customers and reduce their expenses to maintain the status quo. Although they try every possible means, they are ultimately unable to sustain themselves, because rent is too high, accounting for a large portion of their expenses. The meager profits they earn through cheap sales are all used to pay rent, and they are still worried about not having enough. Or, because they are unable to pay the rent, their businesses are sealed up and unable to reopen, which is also common. This is all because the rent is too high, which is a major reason for not being able to restore prosperity. The shops along Caishi Road and Route Paul Beau, which belong to this delegation, are all in a precarious situation due to the high rent. Recently, the French tram company has been repairing the roads for no reason, and the accumulation of mud and soil has blocked traffic. The shops that already have sluggish business are now facing this unexpected blow, which makes it even more difficult to sustain. We have no choice but to ask the landlords to understand. Therefore, the shops on Caishi Road and Route Paul Beau, forced by the environment, have passed a resolution at the general meeting of all shop representatives to elect representatives to form this delegation, and have decided on the following rent reduction standards: (1) For the six months of May, June, July, August, September, and October this year, due to road construction, please landlords reduce the original rent by 50%. (2) From November onwards, collect 70% of the rent. (3) Once the market improves, the original rent will be restored immediately. The above measures have been unanimously approved and submitted to this delegation to request each landlord to voluntarily implement them. It has been found that the rent of your valuable shop houses on Caishi Road and Route Paul Beau is indeed expensive. This special letter is to inform you that we hope that your valuable landlord will deeply understand the difficult times and immediately implement the above rent reduction measures to maintain the market and prevent public resentment.

French Concession Rickshaw Pullers Petition the Municipal Council Today; The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Accepts the Request and Sends Representatives to Accompany Them

According to Xin Sheng She, there are a total of 17,000 public rickshaws in the French Concession (in addition to the 9,990 licenses in the International Settlement). There are approximately 50,000 to 60,000 rickshaw pullers who depend on this for their livelihood. The French Municipal Council is also implementing rickshaw puller registration because the International Settlement is holding rickshaw puller registration. As rickshaw pullers are unwilling to register, the Municipal Council announced that registration will be compulsory from August 1. All the rickshaw pullers are quite dissatisfied with this. On the afternoon of the 28th, a meeting was held in the wasteland of South Wharf, attended by more than 90 representatives, chaired by Shi Changsheng. The resolutions were: 1. Unanimously oppose registration; 2. Send representatives to petition the guild.

Representatives Petition

At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, the rickshaw pullers specially dispatched representatives Shi Changsheng, Zhao Shujing, Zhou Yongcai, Yang Fenghao, Yang Yougui, and others, with a written petition, to the Rickshaw Pullers' Guild in Sanminfang. The standing committee member of the guild, Song Yaokun, received them. The rickshaw puller representatives first stated that the representative meeting had resolved to inform the rickshaw pullers to refuse registration. If the owners want to force registration, they would rather give up the life of pulling rickshaws and requested that justice be upheld. The guild representative agreed to reply after discussion.

Chamber of Commerce Mediation

At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the guild specially dispatched representatives Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, Yu Dajin, and others, with a written petition, to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. They first stated that the rickshaw pullers absolutely oppose registration, and the French Municipal Council’s announcement also ordered the owners to force the rickshaw pullers to register. If the rickshaw pullers do not apply for registration within the deadline, the vehicles will be detained and returned after the rickshaw pullers register. The owners really cannot bear this responsibility. The clerk of the Commerce Section, Yuan Hongjun, received them and promised to accompany them to the French Municipal Council tomorrow (today) to request a change of the method. The guild has appointed Song Yaokun, Zhang Huaiyang, and Yu Dajin as representatives to go to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM and accompany the Chamber of Commerce representatives to petition the French Municipal Council.

Major Fire at Yangjia Ferry, Pudong; Three to Four Hundred Straw Sheds Burned Down Within Two Hours; Over a Thousand Disaster Victims Crying Along the Road

At 8:30 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out in the Nan Shou Beifan Nitantang area of Yangjia Ferry, Pudong. Within two hours, three to four hundred straw sheds were burned down, and more than a thousand people were affected, a true disaster. The details are recorded below. Repeated Fires It is found that the Caonitang area is divided into north and south, separated by the Xiaobang River. The buildings in both places are straw sheds built by people from other provinces. In the past six or seven years, there have been three major fires, each time destroying hundreds of straw sheds, causing superstitious people to regard it as a fiery place. However, after each disaster, the situation soon returned to its original state, because these people from other provinces have nowhere else to live and take the Caonitang area as the basis of their lives.

Sudden Fire Again At 8:30 PM yesterday, the straw houses were all flammable, and in an instant, the fire became a prairie fire, impossible to control. After Yang Zhongquan, the director of the Yangjia Ferry Police Station, heard the report, he urgently telegraphed various fire departments for assistance and dispatched police officers Lin and Yang to the fire scene to maintain order. Soon, Zhao Longsheng, director of the Pudong District Fire Association, drove his men to the scene to put out the fire, but the Xiaobang River was at low tide, and no water could be found nearby, leaving the firefighters helpless. After negotiation, the Dadeshin Oil Factory in the north agreed to provide water, and after connecting a few lengths of hose, water was finally obtained.

Burning Dozens of Acres At this time, fire trucks from Yangjing Town Fire Association, Wu Yi Zhan, Lao Bei Du, and other places all gathered at the scene to assist, but the flames became more and more fierce. In addition, the southeast wind was quite strong, and several dragons of water were ineffective. Moreover, the hoses of the Pudong District and Yangjing Town broke several times due to excessive water pressure, making it more difficult. The fire continued to burn until about 10:30 PM. The area of the fire was even wider than the previous few times. It is estimated that it extended east to the intersection of Fukang Road, south to the riverside, west to the foot of the Taikai wall, and north to the tile houses of Xiechang East and West Lane, covering an area of several tens of acres. All the straw sheds in the area were swept away. Fortunately, the firefighters did their best to protect the tile houses in Xiechang Lane, and the fire could not spread and subsided. Otherwise, if the fire spread to the north, the consequences would be even more unimaginable.

Sounds of Lamentation After the fire broke out, nearby residents, supporting the old and carrying the young, rescued their belongings. Fortunately, no one was injured, but the fire scene was full of winding paths, which were extremely difficult to walk. In addition, the onlookers blocked the way. Fortunately, the police maintained order effectively, and the disaster victims walked out along Fukang Road, Daqing Street, and Caonitang Road in several places. The sounds of lamentation along the way were endless, and the situation was extremely miserable.

Cause Unknown The cause of the fire and which family was responsible is still unknown because the fire broke out suddenly and the police station in charge was unable to determine it for the time being. It is only known that a foreman named Wu is suspected, but it is difficult to confirm. Director Yang was afraid that the arsonist would escape to other places, so after the fire was extinguished, he first brought Wang to the station for questioning.

Relief Measures The fire lasted for about two hours and destroyed about three to four hundred straw sheds, affecting more than a thousand people. Most of them are civilians from other provinces, mostly working as coolies at the docks, extremely poor. After their homes were destroyed, most of them will have nowhere to live, so relief measures are very urgent. It is reported that Director Yang will still follow the previous disaster relief methods and consult with various Shanghai charities for relief.
