Since the Shanghai Municipal Government established the Civilian Welfare Committee, it has been actively planning for civilian welfare projects. The first project to be implemented is civilian housing. The civilian housing on Qimei Road has been contracted by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works and construction has begun. It is expected to be completed by the end of September and leased to civilians. Lumber Industry in the French Concession Resolves to Oppose Sanitary Tax; Representatives Appointed to Petition

The lumber merchants in the French Concession received a notice from the French Municipal Council that each lumber company must apply for a classified business sanitary license and pay a review fee of ten yuan, etc. The lumber companies believe that they have been operating for many years, and the cancellation has been strongly advocated by the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association. At a time when the market is extremely depressed and shops are unable to sustain themselves, they must pay for the license, which is difficult to accept. Therefore, they jointly sent a letter to the guild, requesting it to forward it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for relief, and also requested the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association and the Citizens' Federation to uphold justice and demand that the French authorities strive to cancel the tax. It is now learned that each lumber company suddenly received a notice from a Westerner a few days ago, stating that they should apply for the license from the bureau this week, otherwise the police station will be notified for punishment. Each lumber company was very frightened, so at 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, they convened a temporary emergency meeting of each lumber company at the Citizens' Association on Route Paul Beau to discuss countermeasures. Attendees included Tongyu, Fuxing, Lida, Hongda, Hetai, Yinji, Chengda, Lixing, Zhengda, Xietai, Wanfeng, Maosheng, and more than thirty other companies. Tongyu's Lin Zhengtang was elected as chairman to report on the efforts to seek assistance from all parties, and to report on the subsequent notice from the Westerner that the police station would punish them, and how to deal with it, and asked everyone to discuss it. After the representatives of each industry expressed their opinions, they decided on countermeasures: (1) This industry has never paid taxes, and the attachment table of the classified business regulations does not have any regulations for this industry. The cancellation has also been negotiated before. All of these are proofs that this industry should not pay for the license, and it is decided to deny it to the end. Any oppression will not be recognized, and everyone will sign on the spot to express their determination. (2) Lin Zhengtang and Huang Zhixian were appointed as representatives to petition the relevant national bodies for relief at a fixed time when necessary. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Shareholder of Tongqing Exchange Discovers Manager Embezzling More Than 500,000; Reports to Police Station; Manager Xia Guichu and Others Arrested; Court Opened Trial Yesterday to Obtain Evidence of Fraud

Tongqing Exchange at No. 180 Ningbo Road is a financial giant jointly established by Xu Liantang, Qin Xianfu, Qin Xianfu, Li Hongquan, etc. Each share is valued at 30,000 yuan in national currency. It opened in the spring of the Republic of China in the 13th year. Xia Guichu from Ningbo was hired as manager, and Zhu Haichu from Huzhou was hired as assistant manager. Since its opening, it has suffered huge losses. Recently, after the shareholders checked the accounts, they discovered that Xia and Zhu had major fraud and embezzled public funds. The total amount reached 534,393.23 yuan. Therefore, they entrusted Lawyer Eson to report to the Chief Patrol Room. The police station requested the First Special District Court to sign an arrest warrant. A Chinese detective named Chen Yaoting was sent to Tongqing Exchange to arrest Xia and Zhu. They were temporarily detained. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Division 1 of the Special Court. Defendant Xia Guichu hired lawyers Fan Gang and Zhao Fuding, and Zhu Haichu hired lawyers Wu Linkun and Wang Shudong as defenders. Tongqing Exchange, accompanied by Lawyer Eson, filed a civil suit. First, the police lawyer Jiang Baokang stated that the police station, after receiving the reporter's report, requested the court to issue an arrest warrant and arrested the two on the previous day. Now the police station is prosecuting them for the crime under Article 335 of the Criminal Law. The following is a brief statement of the defendants' crimes: (1) From October 30th last year to July 29th this year, Xia Guichu obtained public bonds of 100,000, 50,000, and 692,000 yuan from the chief accountant Dong Jinghong on three occasions, with receipts, as capital for his private speculative business. (2) In July last year, Xia used the name of Taiji in Ningbo to mortgage 100,000 yuan to Tongqing. Now, including interest, he owes 103,950.73 yuan. It is found that Taiji is actually Xia's alias. Xia also mortgaged a package of square receipts worth 8,393 yuan to Tongqing for a loan of 96,607 yuan. (3) At the end of last year, Taichang, Tongyu, and Xinyuan deposited public bonds worth 157,660 yuan to Tongqing. When they came to retrieve them in March this year, the public bonds were missing. Tongqing compensated them with public bonds of the same value. However, it is still being investigated whether the public bonds were actually deposited or taken by the defendant. (4) A Ruizhi client mortgaged public bonds with a face value of 20,000 yuan to Tongqing for 12,000 yuan. The public bonds were also cashed in by Xia. In summary, the total amount of funds embezzled by the defendants is 534,393.23 yuan. The defendants also confessed in the police station. Then, the Tongqing shareholders stated that they had three shares in Tongqing, totaling 90,000 yuan, but due to the defendants' fraud, each share now requires about 300,000 yuan, causing all shareholders to be ruined and their property mortgaged in order to repay the external debts. Tongqing opened in the spring of the 23rd year, and all the staff in the store belonged to the defendants, so it was difficult to detect the fraud in the accounts. Lawyer Wu Linkan then asked about the manager's authority. The reply was that according to the custom of the money industry, the manager has dictatorial powers, that is, even the shareholders cannot interfere with his duties or check the accounts. Lawyer Zhao Fuding also asked Wang whether the store had set up two supervisors, Wang Zhongyun and Qin Xianfu, to supervise the manager's accounts, but Wang denied it. Questioning Xia Guichu's confession, the plaintiff's accusations were entirely losses from buying and selling public bonds, not embezzlement by us. The public bonds deposited by Taichang and other three companies were sold during the financial crisis to maintain the store's operations. As for the several accounts under my name, it was because the money industry was extremely panicked at the end of last year, and the store's losses were too great. If it was clearly recorded in the accounts, the news would spread to the outside world and inevitably lead to a run on the store. Therefore, after consulting with the supervisors, a portion of the accounts was temporarily transferred to my account as a cover. After the crisis subsided, the accounts would be transferred back, etc. Zhu Haichu confessed that the full authority in the store belonged to the manager, and I had no right to interfere. I resigned from the position of assistant manager at the end of last year. Now I am only assisting in collecting accounts and am not paid. I sometimes knew about Xia Guichu's buying and selling of public bonds, but I did not advise him, etc. The defendants' lawyers then requested permission to post bail. After verifying the confession, Criminal Division Chief Feng Shide decided to postpone the trial for a week. Zhu Haichu was allowed to stop detention with a cash bail of 100,000 yuan or a guarantee of the equivalent amount. Xia Guichu was remanded in custody.

Gang Fight in Zhabei; Iron Bars, Axes, and Sharp Knives Used; Three People Seriously Injured and Sent to the General Bureau

At about 10:00 PM the night before last, dozens of gangsters in the Sun Temple area of Zhabei engaged in a gang fight, each holding iron bars, axes, sharp knives, etc. Police Officer Tang Zijiu of the Sun Temple Police Station No. 40 noticed this and immediately rushed to the station. Inspector Zhang Zhongde then led Police Chief Hu Lianbo, Zhu Liming, Yang Jintang, and others to the scene. When the gangsters saw the police, they fled in all directions. As a result, Zhang Gongqi, Zhang Yongsheng, and Wang A'bao, who were seriously injured, were arrested. Several iron bars found on the roadside were brought back to the station. Inspector Zhang briefly questioned them and then sent them to the Xinzha Sub-bureau. After questioning by Bureau Member Huang Chongren, Zhang Gongqi stated that he was 45 years old, from Henan, and lived at No. 551 Haichang Road. Yesterday (the day before last), Zhang Yongsheng and the owner of the Jin Yu Ji Steel Workshop at the location had a fight. At that time, the steel workshop owner lost. I and someone named Wang came out to mediate. Wang suggested making tea and buying two plasters. I suggested setting up two tables of wine. Later, there was no result. Zhang Yongsheng stated that he was 19 years old, from Changzhou, and lived on Yongxing Xiaoma Road, without knowing the address. This fight was because the copper workshop owner worships the old man Zhang Gongqi. He, as the old man, must save face, so he insisted on setting up twenty tables of wine. Because I could not agree to this condition, he threatened to make me regret it. As a result, yesterday (the day before yesterday), he led many people, each carrying weapons, and beat me, and stabbed my leg several times. Wang A'bao confessed that he was 27 years old, from Suzhou, lived at No. 10 Qia Yu Li, Zhongxing Road, and worked as an electrician. Zhang Gongqi was helping his apprentice. He demanded not only ten tables, but also that Zhang Yongsheng sing for three days. Zhang Yongsheng could not do it, and he said I was not giving him face, so he invited many people to break my head with weapons. After Huang verified, both sides had serious injuries. Zhang Gongqi had severe injuries to his face and arms. Zhang Yongsheng had injuries to both legs, with a total of four stab wounds. Wang A'bao had injuries to his head and hands. They were immediately sent to Shanzhong Hospital for treatment, and the three, Zhang Gongqi, Zhang Yongsheng, and Wang A'bao, together with an iron bar, were sent to the Public Security General Bureau for interrogation.

Gambling Den Case Cracked at the Oriental Hotel; Many Gamblers are Reputable Merchants; Boss Zhang Gengsheng Sentenced to Three Months

Yao Jiaquan, the Chinese detective of the Lao Zha Patrol Room, recently received a tip that there was a large-scale gambling den in Room 307 of the Oriental Hotel, 308 Nanjing West Road, profiting from commissions. The gamblers were all reputable merchants, and the stakes were very high. Detective Yao secretly arrested them and arrested the boss Zhang Gengsheng, as well as gamblers Yang Shukang (real estate businessman) from Shanghai, Xiong Mingde from Nanhui, Shao Yaochen (cotton yarn industry) from Wuxi, and Mrs. Yang Dong (the manager of the Rong Binggen Fuxin Flour Factory), etc. There was also a prostitute named Xue Laoba from Suzhou, who was smoking opium, who was also arrested. The mahjong tiles, dominoes, chips, account books, and opium smoking paraphernalia were all confiscated and brought back to the patrol room. Zhang Gengsheng and the opium smoker Xue Laoba were detained separately. The rest were released on bail of 100 yuan each. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to Criminal Division 1 of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Jiang Baokang explained the situation and prosecuted Zhang Gengsheng based on Article 168 of the Criminal Law and Articles 6 and 10 of the Opium Prohibition Law. Zhang Gengsheng confessed that the room was opened by him, but only mahjong was played and no opium was sold. When questioned, Yang Shukang, Xiong Mingde, Sun Yanru, and Shao Yaochen all confessed to playing mahjong. Xue Laoba denied smoking opium, and Mrs. Yang Dong also denied participating in gambling. After verifying the confessions, Chief Judge Feng Shide sentenced Zhang Gengsheng to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 50 yuan. Xue Laoba was fined 15 yuan. Yang Shukang, Xiong Mingde, Sun Yanru, and Shao Yaochen were each fined 20 yuan. Mrs. Yang Dong was acquitted. All gambling and opium paraphernalia were confiscated.

The Bureau of Social Affairs and the Bureau of Public Safety Jointly Prohibit Da Jiao

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs believes that in Shanghai, every year between July and August, idlers initiate the Yu Lan Pen Festival (commonly known as Da Jiao) on various roads and lanes, soliciting money from house to house, promoting superstition, and wasting people's money and harming their wealth. At a time when the floods in various provinces are terrible and the victims are in dire need of rescue, it is not appropriate to waste hard-earned money on useless consumption. It is necessary to ban the practice to reverse the bad trend. A few days ago, the Bureau sent personnel to consult with the Bureau of Public Safety. In addition to the joint announcement by the two bureaus, the Bureau of Public Safety also issued orders to all subordinate units to strictly prohibit the practice.

Minghua Bank Lawsuit Heard Again Yesterday: Tong Jinhui Denies Being Chairman; Plaintiff Requests Inspection of Records

Minghua Bank, located at Henan Road, Beijing Road, suddenly declared its closure in May of this year due to unfavorable market conditions. The First Special Court has already held two hearings, but due to the defendants' absence, the court ordered a postponement. All of this has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Zhao of the Eighth Criminal Division continued the hearing. Only Tong Jinhui and Yu Dehua appeared in court. Miao Zhenfan's lawyer, Wang Fu, presented a telegram stating that manager Zhang Gangbo was currently being detained by the Qingdao Municipal Government. Miao Zhenfan was unable to return to Shanghai because of the busy affairs of the Qingdao branch and requested a postponement. Tong Jinhui denied being the chairman or a director. The defendant's lawyer, Zhu Hongru, stated that after Minghua closed, all important account books were listed and entrusted to accountant Xu Yongzuo and his law firm, Wei Jiong, for safekeeping. Although Minghua Bank repeatedly convened shareholder meetings from 1931 to this year, they all failed due to insufficient attendance to form a quorum. Therefore, since a shareholders' meeting never convened, there were no board members elected. Judge Yang stated that because the defendants were not all present, the case would be postponed. Journalists' Association Aids Xuzhou Xin Wan Bao

The Shanghai Journalists' Association, in order to assist the Xuzhou Xin Wan Bao, resolved in its fourth standing committee meeting to write to the Fourth Branch of the High Court, requesting a fair trial. This has been reported previously. The letter from the association to the Fourth Branch of the High Court is as follows:

Respected Sirs,

We received a letter from Xia Yiming, deputy editor-in-chief of the Xuzhou Xin Wan Bao, stating that their newspaper was sealed by the Ninth District Security Command of Jiangsu Province on June 27th because it published a telegram from a Nanjing newspaper. Editor-in-chief Chen Suyi was detained and sentenced to seven months' imprisonment by the Tongshan County Government, which also handles judicial affairs, on June 30th. An appeal has now been filed. They request our assistance. After discussion at the fourth standing committee meeting, we believe that if the Xin Wan Bao merely reprinted news of "reactionary leaflets appearing in Ping City" from a Nanjing newspaper, then both newspapers are operated by Chinese people and are under the jurisdiction of the central government. It is unlikely that news from a newspaper under central control would constitute a crime if reprinted in a local newspaper. Furthermore, the Tongshan County Government's interrogation and judgment, conducted on a weekend holiday, one day before the establishment of the court, seem to be biased. Since this case has been appealed to your court, we urge you to conduct a fair trial to conform to justice and sentiment.

Sincerely,

The Standing Committee of the Shanghai Journalists' Association

Yan Duhe, Tang Shichang, Jiang Songdao, Jiang Xiangqing, Wang Xinming, Jiang Hongjiao, Zhu Zian.

Miao Horen Angered by Wife's Infidelity, Shoots and Wounds Paramour; Police Prosecute for Attempted Murder; Miao Chen Admits Adultery

Miao Horen, a local resident, 38 years old, runs the "Xianrentang" at 236 North Fujian Road, offering medical treatments. On the 27th of this month, at 5:45 AM, Miao, suspecting his wife, Chen (also known as Lin Di), of having an improper relationship with Wang Lianji, a worker at the copper shop next door at 232 North Fujian Road, became enraged. He secretly took a pistol, lured Wang to Yushun Lane on Qipu Road, and shot him, wounding him in the right flank. The International Settlement Police learned of the incident. Detective Shang Wu, along with detectives Zheng Huaili and Li Wenbin, arrested Miao Horen, seizing a pistol and six bullets. The injured Wang Lianji was taken to the Douren Hospital, where doctors found a bullet wound in his right flank and surgically removed the bullet. He was hospitalized for treatment. Yesterday morning, the police prosecuted Miao Horen in the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court for attempted murder under Article 27, Section 1 of the Criminal Law. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu presented the case, stating that the defendant was arrested after being reported by the victim, Wang Lianji. During the investigation, the police asked where the gun was hidden. The defendant led them to the home of Sun Rusong at 768 Tianmu Road, where the gun was found hidden inside a shoe cabinet. Sun was not home at the time. Sun's mother stated that Sun was at 580 Lane 14, Weihaiwei Road, on business. The defendant had secretly placed the gun under the bed that morning, and her son was not yet awake, so she was unaware. The police arrested Sun but released him after determining he was not involved. The defendant confessed that he bought the gun from Jin Fushou, who lived on North Fujian Road five years ago. The police arrested Jin, but Jin denied selling the gun, claiming he was being framed. After investigation, the police released Jin as well. The defendant also confessed that because Wang Lianji had an affair with his wife and had secret meetings with her, he plotted to lure Wang out on the pretext of repairing a glass cabinet and shot him in Yushun Lane. Wang is still in the hospital. The case was then postponed, and the gun and bullets were presented as evidence. Questioned, Miao Horen stated that he bought the gun from Jin Fushou for 100 yuan five years ago when he lived on North Fujian Road for self protection as he had once been robbed. He runs the "Xianrentang" on North Fujian Road, treating children's illnesses. Wang Lianji is a worker at the neighboring copper shop. In the past half month, he has been having an affair with my wife, frequently going out together, causing scandalous rumors. For the sake of my reputation, I arranged to meet Wang the previous morning to negotiate. When we arrived at Yushun Lane, I reasoned with Wang, but Wang not only refused to listen but also said that my wife was willingly participating in the affair. Enraged, I drew my gun to scare him. I don't know how, but the bullet went off. I didn't realize Wang had been hit and went home. Later, Wang incited seven or eight colleagues from the shop, all armed, to beat me, causing me to be injured all over. I had no intention of murdering Wang.

Miao Chen, the defendant's wife, stated that she is from Funing, 30 years old, has been married to the defendant for eight years, and has two children. Their relationship was usually harmonious. She admitted to having an affair with Wang Lianji for only about ten days.

Judge Liu Guigui reviewed the statements and ordered the defendant to be detained for seven days before the next hearing.

Page 11

After Scientific Identification, Concealed Inheritance Revealed; Confirmed Not to be Zhou Songqing's Handwriting; Huang Xianyao Confesses the Truth; Written by Wu Jiajin, Clerk of Lawyer Mi Jingshen

After Huang Chujiu, founder of the Gongfa Company, died on January 19th of the tenth year of the Republic, the Riyue Bank, Dashijie, and Youlan Beichubu, all under the Gongfa Company, simultaneously went bankrupt. Creditors filed lawsuits, and Huang's family declared bankruptcy, handing over all private property to repay debts and requesting the court to grant the family a living allowance of 40,000 yuan. Eventually, over 20% of the debt was repaid, and the funds were managed by the First Special Court. After four years, the debt remains unsettled due to complicated matters. In the spring of this year, Wang Shaozeng, a creditor of Gongfa Company, discovered that Huang Chujiu had

Concealed a Large Inheritance

after his death, deposited at the residence of Zhou Songqing, Huang Chuli's father-in-law, at 52 Qiaojiabang, Huajie. Zhou issued a receipt stating, "After the matter is settled, the 100,000 yuan allocated to Xianyao's (Huang Xianyao's) household will be returned to their management." The receipt was signed "Songqing" and contained a handwritten fingerprint. The receipt was stored in a safe deposit box at Guohua Bank and Huang Xianyao based on this receipt, petitioned the Shanghai District Court for mediation in September of the twenty-second year, requesting Zhou Songqing to return the property. Because

Mediation Failed

and Huang had not formally filed a lawsuit, Wang Shaozeng, believing that Zhou Songqing and Huang Xianyao, father and son-in-law, were engaging in actions to damage the interests of creditors, hired lawyer Xu Yannian to file a criminal self-lawsuit in the Second Special Court against Huang Xianyao and Zhou Songqing for damaging creditor rights. After the court repeatedly summoned them, only Zhou Songqing appeared and denied issuing the receipt, while Huang Xianyao consistently failed to appear. The court issued an arrest warrant, and police officers arrested Huang on June 14th. During the hearing the next day, Huang stated that he found the receipt

Inside His Wife's Wardrobe

between March and April of the twenty-first year. He had petitioned the District Court for mediation, but it failed, and his father-in-law denied the matter. After investigation, it was confirmed that no such property existed. Zhou Songqing requested to retrieve the receipt and authenticate its veracity. On June 21st, the court summoned both parties to open the safe deposit box at Guohua Bank and retrieve the receipt. It matched the photograph submitted by the plaintiff, Wang Shaozeng. Zhou Songqing still denied everything, claiming Huang Xianyao had forged it. He reported it to the police, requesting an investigation. When the Second Special Court continued the hearing on the case of damaging creditor rights on June 26th, several creditors of Gongfa Company joined the lawsuit. Huang Xianyao stated to the court that when he was detained and awaiting bail, someone had

Forced and Enticed

him to write a receipt. During the police investigation, he was ordered to write characters, fearing further complications, he requested the court's attention. Judge Shu Chang believed that the evidence needed to be investigated, he postponed the hearing and ordered Zhou and Huang to each post 30,000 yuan in bail. Zhou was released, but Huang, unable to pay bail, was detained in the Second Special Court's detention center.

During this period, the police compared Zhou and Huang's writing on the receipt to the characters on the discovered 100,000 yuan receipt. Rao Boze, deputy chief of police, a calligraphy expert, magnified and photographed samples of the writing and then

Scientifically

analyzed and identified it, concluding that the receipt was not written by Zhou Songqing. Huang Xianyao confessed to the police that the receipt was written by Wu Jiajin, a clerk at lawyer Mi Jingshen's office. Yesterday, Huang Xianyao, Mi Jingshen, and Wu Jiajin were sent to the Second Special Court. Judge Li Changnian of the First Criminal Division conducted the hearing. (The second defendant, Mi Jingshen, had left the bar, though his residence was at 12 Dada Lane, Avenue Haig. The third defendant, Wu Jiajin, was living at 2 Xinjiang Road, Zhabei. Neither could be located.) Huang, 31 years old, from Yuyao, was charged according to Article 210 of the Criminal Law, as was explained by police lawyer Fei Xizhen, who presented a large volume of

Enlarged Handwriting Photographs.

The judge questioned Huang, who confessed that the receipt was written by Wu Jiajin from lawyer Mi Jingshen's office. "I was not instructed to do it; I was deceived. The matter arose because I wanted to request my wife to cohabitate with me. Lawyer Mi said that cohabitation was pointless; it would be better to get some money from my father-in-law. He offered to help me find a way and had Wu write this receipt to request mediation. Later, because mediation failed, I no longer wanted it. Then a Mr. Tang (Zengshou) used this receipt to blackmail me. When that failed, he put the receipt in the safe deposit box, causing the creditors to report me." At this point, the court postponed the hearing to August 7th at 8:00 AM because the plaintiff, Zhou Songqing, was not present. The defendants were ordered to be summoned again for questioning. The defendant was remanded to detention.

Northern District National Goods Fair Opened Yesterday; Party Representatives Raised Flag and Opened Fair; Temporary Market Fully Open Yesterday

The Northern District National Goods Fair, sponsored by the Shanghai Chinese National Goods Association, held its opening ceremony yesterday at 4:00 PM at the association's grounds at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Zhajiang Road in Zhabei. Details are as follows:

Chairman's Report

Those present yesterday included Party Representative Zhu Yangwu, Fan Zhongzhang from Guangdong Brothers Rubber Company, Fan Guanghan from Yaxin Fragrance Company, Xu Zihou from Sancai Factory, and over 300 guests from various sectors. After Chairman Sun Yu conducted the ceremony, the chairman gave a report on the purpose of the fair, stating that the association, recognizing that Zhabei had not recovered from the scars of the January 28th Incident and that imports of foreign goods were increasing daily, causing alarming financial losses, organized the Northern District National Goods Fair to encourage citizens to use domestic goods. He was pleased that guests had braved the heat to participate in today's opening. The national goods movement has been promoted for many years, but with limited success. In this time of national crisis, he hoped that patriotic compatriots would use and promote domestic goods to develop the national goods industry and achieve the goals of saving the country and saving ourselves. Chairman Sun Yu then delivered a response (omitted).

Representative Speeches

Party Representative Zhu Yangwu then gave a speech, stating that the significance of the National Goods Fair was to concentrate the products of manufacturers on one hand and to make the people of northern Shanghai aware of domestic goods and to promote them on the other, to lay the foundation for saving the country. In recent years, imports of foreign goods have increased daily, with financial outflows amounting to hundreds of millions, weakening the nation's foundations and leaving it with little room to stand in the future, which is truly painful. Now, if we want to stop these financial losses and save ourselves from danger, we must use domestic goods. He hoped that everyone would promote and correct this, and that manufacturers would improve their products and dedicate themselves to domestic goods and strive for the country.

Market Opens

After the speeches, the military band led Mr. Zhu to the gate, where the national flag was raised and the curtain outside the gate was drawn back. The crowd cheered and rushed in. The association's temporary market immediately opened for business. To entertain the guests, the association hired a full troupe of Gujin performers to perform various acts. Yesterday's attendance was exceptionally high.

At 9:50 PM last night, the Jiangsu Automobile Company at 125 Guizhou Road received a call to rent a car. The caller, claiming to be a Mr. Li from Room 412 of the Great Shanghai Hotel on Xiangfen Lane, requested the immediate dispatch of a car, saying he was waiting at the entrance of the Great Shanghai. The company's accountant immediately ordered driver Zhu Alin to take taxi No. 17691 (International Settlement) / 4181 (Chinese Territory). Upon arrival, three well-dressed men, all around 30 years old, were waiting at the entrance. Upon seeing the car, they immediately got in and told the driver to drive east along Nanjing Road towards the Bund. When the car reached the back of Wills and Sons, one of them ordered the car to stop. Two men remained in the car while one got out and told the driver to park on Renji Road. The one who had left went into the He Shideng Western Restaurant at 20 Nanjing Road for about 15 minutes. Then, the first man returned with three others, hurrying out. Reaching the car, one of them pulled out a gun and forced the driver out of the car. The driver had no choice but to comply. One of the men then started the engine and drove away. The driver, realizing he had encountered robbers, immediately reported to the company by phone. The accountant immediately reported to the Laozao Police Station. However, since the incident occurred in the jurisdiction of the Central Police Station, the driver was instructed to personally report to the Central Police Station. At this time, the He Shideng Restaurant also came to report that three or four robbers had broken into the restaurant and displayed guns. Three diners were present and were robbed of over 300 yuan in silver dollars. The police chief, upon receiving the report, immediately telegraphed the relevant police stations, the French Concession police, and the Public Security Sub-Bureau to be on the lookout for the car. However, as of press time, the car had not been recovered.

Xu Xiaochu Talks About Reasons for Establishing Narcotics Management Office: Department of Health Adopted Request from Leye Association

Xin Sheng News reports that Mr. Xu Xiaochu, a standing committee member of the Xin Leye Trade Association, commented on the process of the Central Department of Health establishing a narcotics management office in Shanghai as follows: Since Chairman Chiang issued a strict ban on potent narcotics last year, merchants needing to purchase narcotics for formulation purposes have complied with the Central Management of Pharmaceutical Merchants Regulations and Chairman Chiang's directives without error. Foreign merchants, however, are not subject to these restrictions and can import freely with consular certification. Therefore, when representatives of the Xin Yaoye Trade Association and the Pharmaceutical Factory Trade Association went to Beijing twice to petition for the Management of Prepared Medicines Regulations, they repeatedly requested that Director Liu of the Department of Health establish a special office to regulate and manage narcotics. Director Liu adopted this request, so the establishment of the management office was in response to this request. Reports stating that pharmacies are prohibited from selling narcotics are a misunderstanding.

Ye Bocang Evaluates Fortunes to Aid Disaster Relief

Ye Bocang, a native of Wu, has lived in Shanghai for many years. In his spare time, he enjoys studying fortune-telling and provides evaluations and guidance to those who are lost. His words are often accurate, and friends and relatives who have consulted him are amazed at his abilities. However, he usually does not accept fees, except for close friends and relatives. But during times of disaster, he uses his knowledge to help the public and donates his earnings to disaster relief. In the past, during the disasters of 1925 and 1931, Mr. Ye's fortune-telling and disaster relief efforts were very successful. This summer, the heavy rains in Hubei, Shandong, Hunan, and Jiangxi Provinces have caused flooding and unprecedented disasters. Mr. Ye, feeling compassion, is again publicly evaluating fortunes to aid in charitable efforts, despite the heat. Those who seek evaluation will not only learn about their fortune and avoid misfortune but also benefit disaster victims. This is a win-win situation and a great merit. The fee for a brief evaluation is 5 yuan, and for a detailed evaluation, it is 10 yuan. Disaster relief donations can be sent to Xintong Bank, 579 Henan Road, and will be delivered within a week without delay. If you donate to the flood relief and note that it is for "Bocang's Fortune-Telling Disaster Relief," it can also be exchanged.

7. Proposal on how to regulate the association's area of jurisdiction. Resolved: West to Hongkou Creek, east to Linqing Road.

9. Committee member Du proposed that the heads of each department and the newly appointed standing committee members should be officially appointed and photographed. Resolved: To be held this Saturday afternoon.

10. Proposal for the association's regular meetings. Resolved: Regular meetings will be held at 8:00 PM every Thursday.

11. Proposal for regular joint meetings of rent reduction associations in all districts of Shanghai. Resolved: Committee member Du will contact them separately, and a date will be announced later.

12. Proposal on how often the association's executive committee should meet. Resolved: To meet on the 1st and 15th of each month. The meeting adjourned around 5:00 PM.

Dunhe Lane Rent Reduction Meeting

Dunhe Lane on Route Ratard in the French Concession was built around October of the 20th year of the Republic (1931). The location is in the west and not a prosperous commercial area. Commerce has always been sluggish here, especially since the January 28th Shanghai Incident. Shops have become even more desolate, with few customers. Coupled with high rents that are unbearable, tenants have united to form the Dunhe Lane branch of the 8th District Subcommittee of the Second Special District Citizens' Federation. Yesterday at 4 p.m., the second preparatory meeting was held at the 8th District Subcommittee's office. Despite the scorching sun and hot weather, the tenants did not hesitate to attend on time, totaling 27 households. Zhang Zhiqin of Nanchang Company was elected as chairman, and Zhu Yunsheng as secretary. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, the discussion of the rent reduction plan began. (1) At the previous meeting, it was resolved to send a letter to the managing agent, Talley & Co., requesting a 30% rent reduction. The Document Section has already prepared and sent the letter, but after ten days, no response has been received. How should this be handled? After the tenants present expressed their opinions, the chairman summarized the consensus and put it to a vote. It was resolved that if the landlord does not grant a rent reduction, the rent due will be deposited in a designated bank under the name "Talley & Co. Managing Agents," to demonstrate determination until the goal is achieved. Everyone applauded and unanimously approved. (2) To prevent the landlord from suing for rent arrears, it was resolved to hire Wang Peiyuan as legal counsel to legally protect rights and interests. (3) To appoint responsible personnel to prevent the landlord's henchmen, it was resolved to appoint Zhang Zhiqin of Nanchang Company and Zeng Jinchun of Heji as northern supervisors of all tenants, Yongfayuan and Yongqing as central supervisors of all tenants, and Zhang Jiyun and Dayuan as southern supervisors of all tenants. (4) To report to superiors for record-keeping, it was resolved that the Document Section would be responsible. (5) For the next meeting, it was resolved to hold the inaugural meeting at 3 p.m. on August 3rd and to invite party and government agencies to attend and provide guidance. The meeting adjourned.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The report on the 241st inspection of the issuance reserve of Central Bank convertible notes states that, in accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the amount of convertible notes issued and the reserve funds. The 241st inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on July 27, 24th year of the Republic (1935). The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: Silver dollars 10,571,8220, including silver dollar notes 9,876,8250 and subsidiary coin notes 6,949,970. Total amount of convertible note reserve funds: Silver dollars 10,571,8220, including cash reserve of silver dollars 8,185,8220. This cash reserve includes 7,709,8527 in the bank's issuance vault, 2,282,823 in branches in various ports, and 2,476,870 in correspondent banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to silver dollars 23,860,000. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: $373,324.70. Total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve funds: $373,324.70. This reserve includes 7,351 taels, 9 mace, and 5 fen of standard gold, equivalent to customs gold $373,324.70 at the fixed price of 5.0779. In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be guaranteed by legal guaranteed goods. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guaranteed reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby submitted. July 29, 24th year of the Republic of China. Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank: Li Fusun, Supervisors: Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilun.

New Filament Electric Bulb Introduced

The world-renowned electric lamp giants General Electric, Edison, Osram, and Philips have now created a new type of ordinary light bulb with higher efficiency, called the "Woven Filament Bulb." With a wattage of 40 watts, it emits 10% more light than ordinary bulbs while using the same amount of electricity. In other words, users can obtain more light for the same electricity bill. This is a major advance in electrical science. This type of light bulb can reduce the cost of lighting. In ordinary argon bulbs, the filament is surrounded by nitrogen or argon, making it less likely to melt than vacuum bulbs. The filament of the woven filament bulb is even more heat-resistant. Its filament is shorter and thicker. Because the filament is larger, it also emits more light. Although this type of light bulb seems very simple, it is the result of several years of dedicated research before it could be widely applied. It is reported that this type of light bulb is now sold by the Zhonghe Bulb Company in this city, which is the manager of the famous General Electric, Edison, Osram, and Philips legacy light bulbs.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated: Shandong and surrounding areas are cloudy, with winds varying from northeast to southeast. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and clear, with light winds of variable direction. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the coastline of this area are cloudy with showers and strong southeast winds. The East China Sea and surrounding areas of Taiwan have a very intense cyclone, with very bad weather, showers, and storms, due to a hurricane approaching Taiwan from the north-northwest. The hurricane center at noon reached within approximately 60 miles of 23 degrees 30 minutes north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude, with strong winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday, the local temperature was a maximum of 94.1 and a minimum of 78.3. On the same day last year, the maximum was 100.2 and the minimum was 77.4.

Snippets

— (Yu Mugu)

"Everyone knows how to perform magic, but each has their own unique skill." In this world we live in, everything, every moment, is a performance of magic. Because each has its own unique skill, it forms various levels of life styles of wealth, poverty, joy, and sorrow.

Dolls are what children like to play with. In fact, people all like to play with children, so children are people's dolls. And capitalists like to play with people, so people are the capitalists' dolls. Money likes to play with capitalists, and capitalists often become the dolls of money. In short, all people in the world are dolls played by money.

"People's hearts are different, each like their face. But people's faces can be seen clearly with the naked eye. People's hearts cannot be窥探 by the naked eye. One's own face can also be seen in a mirror at a glance, but one's own heart cannot be seen in a mirror. People ignore this principle. If they don't even know what their own heart is like, how can they specialize in blaming people's hearts for being unpredictable?"

The scenes of a movie are projected until the end, causing the audience to have unlimited thoughts and criticisms. Our lives are also like performing a movie, scene after scene passes until the final death, arousing the thoughts and criticisms of many people. Therefore, before we are alive, we must first think about after death, and plan for the thoughts and criticisms of many people.

In Memory of Mr. Yun Tieqiao

— Tian Sheweng

Tian Sheweng said: Writing changes with the times. Du Gu Changzhou, following the decadent elegance of the Six Dynasties, emerged with peace and gentleness. Ouyang, after the turmoil of the Five Dynasties, also emerged with peace; both were enough to save the declining customs. In the late Qing Guangxu years, a few patriots had the ambition to change customs through fiction. Gentlemen such as Wu Yanren, Li Boyuan, Wang Yuansheng, Lin Qinnan, Jiang Jingjian, Chen Lengxue, Bao Tianxiao, and Xu Fumin all used fiction to influence the times. After the cessation of Xiaoshuo Lin, Yuet Yuet Xiaoshuo, and Shangwu Illustrated Fiction, Di Pingzi founded the Xiaoshuo Shibao, and Wang Xishen created the Xiaoshuo Yuebao. This was during the Guangxu and Xuantong periods.

At that time, the Xiaoshuo Shibao published three lengthy novels by the American novelist Charles Garvice, "Nutmeg Flower", "Black-Clad Lady", and "Ripple on the Yinyin", which were charming and sensual and could move my heart. The translator was Mr. Yun Tieqiao of Wujin. After the Qing dynasty was overthrown, Shuo Bao arose, piled up in confusion, and were called the Mandarin Duck Butterfly School, which was criticized by connoisseurs. At that time, Mr. Yun took charge of the selection of the Xiaoshuo Yuebao, corrected the malpractice of piling up, and wrote and translated fiction that was clear and utterly different from the slender and beautiful works such as "Nutmeg Flower" and "Black-Clad Lady." Did he also see that if the lowly pot roars like thunder, and customs are changed, nothing but this could lead to it? At that time, some criticized Mr. Yun's novels as "big sayings." In my opinion, Mr. Yun was truly the Martin Luther of the fiction world at that time.

Mr. Yun, whose given name was Shujue, courtesy name Tieqiao, also known as Lengfeng, Jiaomu, was a native of Wujin, Jiangsu, and a descendant of the Qing painter Nantian Laoren. In the Qing Dynasty, he graduated from Nanyang Public School, so he had a good foundation in Western languages. His translated novels used a clear and beautiful style to express lingering feelings. Readers admired and praised works such as "Nutmeg Flower", "Black-Clad Lady", and "Spring Water from the Mountains". Mr. Yun deeply regretted not knowing medicine because his children were often sick, so he widely studied classical medical texts; after a long time, he gained considerable insights. He was the first to use scientific methods to organize classical medical texts.

Mr. Yun's medical knowledge was profound, and his insights were very rich. After he began practicing medicine, patients who sought his diagnosis recovered quickly, so his threshold was worn through. Mr. Yun immersed himself in medicine, diligently and tirelessly. In his spare time, he entertained himself with writing. To this day, his medical writings form a huge collection; commentators regard him as a medical expert, but they did not know that Mr. Yun was originally a novelist.

Mr. Yun had been ill for a long time. Recently, his illness worsened due to the unbearable heat, and he suddenly passed away the day before yesterday at the age of fifty-eight. After the death of Mr. Zeng Mengpu (East Asian Sick Man) last month, the news of Mr. Yun's death has been heard again. Another novelist has weakened, is it not just the misfortune of the national medical community!

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seventeen: Do Not Ask About the Hidden Pain of a Daughter's Body; Strive to See the Face of a Noble Person and Adore Their High Moral Character

Li Shilian said, "Seeking Buddha and seeking honor, why bother going around in circles? Now that Mr. Zhang has become wealthy, if you let him help you with a small favor, that would be enough." Yang Wanhua laughed, "I have ears, and I have long heard that a central official is coming and is related to him." She turned her eyes to look at Jiefu's face. Jiefu raised his eyebrows and said, "If you want me to think of a little way to help you, it may not be difficult after tomorrow." Wanhua said, "Why does it have to be after tomorrow? Is tomorrow a day to make a big fortune?" Jiefu said, "Didn't you hear that Commissioner Lan is arriving tomorrow? He is my relative. When he comes, he will inevitably have many things for me to do. Naturally, if I am asked to do things, of course, there will be money passing through my hands. At that time, I can move a little small amount for you from the large sums of money. That's not worth mentioning." Wanhua said, "Don't you know that I have to leave early tomorrow morning? If I wait for you to give me the money tomorrow, I won't be able to catch the car to Tongguan, and I will have to spend several more dollars to buy a ticket, which is still not cost-effective." Jiefu smiled faintly, "I am just in the position of a friend, helping a little. How can everything in the world be done perfectly? Then you will have to choose for yourself." Hearing his tone, Wanhua could not get any practical indication, and it seemed that there was not much hope of getting money from him, so she stood there in a daze. Zhang Jiefu seemed to be very busy and did not have time to chat, turned his body, and walked to his own room. Li Shilian closely followed behind and also left. Only Yang Wanhua was left under the corridor. She was able to get a train ticket because of Zhang Jiefu's kind words. Otherwise, Jia Duocai had already gotten Zhu Yueying, and he would cross the river and tear down the bridge, and she would have no way. (277)

Imperial Incense Wanders Around Record

— Originally written by Princess Deling, translated by Qin Shouou

The Yellow River, as everyone knows, is a very unsafe river, and every year it has to cause several major floods; this year, as usual, it has broken out again, and the people along the coast are naturally suffering from famine and epidemics. The number of people drowned is always more than two or three thousand, and there are five or six thousand people who have become homeless. Originally, the court had some preparations for this kind of disaster that had to occur every year, but this year's disaster was particularly serious, and some of the relief funds and food originally prepared were not enough to distribute, which caused the officials handling the relief to be at a loss. There was no way but to report the truth. According to the court's old rules, whatever happens will inevitably be delayed a lot. First, it must be sent to the Military Aircraft Department for reading, and then transferred by the Military Aircraft Department to the relevant yamen for review. After review for a long time, a memorial will be drafted and the imperial decree will be requested; this way, it often takes a month or two to deliver. That day, after the Empress Dowager received the report that the disaster was serious and the relief funds were insufficient, she reversed the old habits and resolutely picked up the pen and wrote a few sentences, and immediately handed it over to the Ministry of Household to urgently allocate hundreds of thousands of taels of silver from the treasury, dedicated to relieving the Huang disaster. She was still afraid that they would not understand her good intentions and would not be very willing, so she issued another special order saying:

"As long as it is really used for disaster relief, we should not save a penny; if there is not enough cash in the treasury and there is no way to allocate it temporarily, I am also willing to donate my private property. We must do this thing to a relatively satisfactory result!" (377)

One-Act Play

Wife's Business

— Yin Yiqiu

Characters: Cheng Caizhen (gold-worshiping woman), Liu Hongxiang (rich merchant), Lao Zhang (court clerk), three judges, two lawyers, two bailiffs, and several spectators

Location: Court

Curtain opens: (Near the start of the trial, Lao Zhang is sitting under the public case. The plaintiff's lawyer walks over to report. The two are acquaintances and chat casually)

Lao Zhang: Lawyer Pan, good morning!

Lawyer: It's time, hasn't the judge arrived yet?

Lao Zhang: He's here, the court will open soon!

Lawyer: Today's case is interesting, a very beautiful woman is asking a very ugly man to admit that she is his wife.

Lao Zhang: I guess this man will definitely admit she is.

Lawyer: If he admitted her, would she still need to sue? Fool!

Lao Zhang: Alas! There are really such unfair things in the world! A beautiful woman is asking to be his wife, and he still won't admit it?

Lawyer: Lao Zhang! Why are you sighing? Haven't you got a wife even at your age?

Lao Zhang: To tell you the truth... my wife was really beautiful, but because I was poor, she ran away with someone six years ago!

Lawyer: Didn't you look for her back then?

Lao Zhang: Because I was looking for her, I went from Beiping to Shanghai. At that time, I was really like a madman, I couldn't tell the taste of tea and rice, and I was always thinking about her!

Lawyer: What happened later?

Lao Zhang: Alas! Don't mention it! Today, it has been exactly six years, and there has been no news at all!

Lawyer: Women change their minds so quickly, I say that woman is too heartless! (Cheng Caizhen enters, Liu Hongxiang and his lawyer enter, spectators enter one after another)

Lao Zhang: The judge is here (everyone stands up to salute, the atmosphere is solemn)

(The judge flips through the files, the bailiff leads Caizhen into the plaintiff's column, Hongxiang stands in the defendant's column, Lao Zhang is sitting directly behind Caizhen, staring at the back of her head in great surprise,)

Judge: Are you called Cheng Caizhen?

Caizhen: Yes.

Judge: How old are you? Where are you from?

Caizhen: Twenty-eight years old, from Beiping!

Judge: Why are you suing Liu Hongxiang?

Caizhen: Because he doesn't admit that I'm his wife!

Judge: When did you marry him?

Caizhen: I married him when I was twenty-two years old, Qiguang, he treated me well, but starting from the winter of the 17th year of the Republic (1928), he became increasingly indifferent to me and abandoned me until now. Now that he has made a fortune, he has lost his conscience and won't let me into his house, please save me, Judge!

Judge: Liu Hongxiang!

Hongxiang: Yes.

Judge: How old are you? Where are you from?

Hongxiang: Thirty-six years old, from Shanghai!

Judge: What business do you do?

Hongxiang: I own a silk shop.

Judge: Did you hear Cheng Caizhen's words just now clearly? What is your opinion?

Hongxiang: I don't admit that she is my wife, because she has never married me! But we had a relationship five years ago. At that time, I was just a shop assistant in a silk shop. She嫌ed I was poor and fell in love with someone else and left. Now that she sees my situation is better, she has come to pester me again, I will never admit it!

(At this moment, all of Lao Zhang's painful past events flood into his mind)

Plaintiff's lawyer: Now the facts have proven that the plaintiff and the defendant have a marital relationship, please the judge to confirm the plaintiff as the defendant's wife!

Defendant's lawyer: According to Article 208 of the Civil Procedure Law, please the judge reject the plaintiff's suit!

Lao Zhang: (emotionally agitated) What a vile woman! (Cheng Caizhen suddenly sees Lao Zhang and is panic-stricken)

Bailiff: Lao Zhang! Are you dizzy? Where is this place?

Lao Zhang: (like a madman) Lawyer Pan! She is my wife! (grabs Caizhen) Come back with me!

Caizhen: Who is your wife?

Lao Zhang: What a heartless woman, I almost died because of you!……

Judge: (enraged) This person is crazy, throw him out!

Caizhen: Judge! I don't know him!

Lao Zhang: (being held by two bailiffs) What a shameless woman! Using business tactics to marry a husband, if the rich are not your customers, you force them! If the poor are clearly your customers, you push them out! I can't eat your meat, but I must peel your skin...

Bailiff: Stop babbling! Get out! Get out! Get out!

Lao Zhang: What if I don't go out?

Bailiff: (strongly pushes Lao Zhang) Scram! Scram! Scram!

Lao Zhang: I just won't go out! I just won't go out!

(A burst of noise)—Curtain closes—

Shanghai International Tennis Rotary Cup Tournament: Five Nations Participating, Schedule Set to Begin August 10th

The Sixth Shanghai International Tennis Rotary Cup Tournament held a meeting yesterday organized by the National Sports Advancement Association at the New Asia Restaurant, gathering representatives from participating nations. Those in attendance included: (England) Pan Liwei Que, (Portugal) Ke Lasha, (America) Tuo Ping, (China) Hu Xiansheng, (Association Representative) Zhou Jiaqi, (Secretary) Shi Kang. Zhou Jiaqi was publicly elected as chairman. After careful discussion, the following resolutions were made and the schedule was set:

(1) The first week of competition will begin on August 10th.

(2) The competition venue will be the Shanghai Tennis Club courts on Kangti Road.

(3) "Slazenger" balls are designated as the official balls for the competition.

(4) Each team should send two referees to officiate this competition.

(5) The competition method will adopt the Davis Cup system, but this year's competition format will be modified to two singles matches on the first day, one doubles match on the second day, and the reverse singles matches on the third day will be cancelled.

(6) The competition schedule is as follows:

(Note) The representatives of each country, considering (1) the heavy schedule of competitions in this port, and (2) that holding competitions on Fridays or Mondays would interfere with the players' professions, decided to cancel the old reverse singles matches to save time. However, the pairing of the first and second singles players should be the responsibility of the leaders of each country during registration, based on the players' skill levels, and the names of the singles players should be listed in order of priority. Once all registrations are collected, the list will be announced and the competition will be held according to the order of registration. If other teams have objections to the arrangement of the singles order, the committee will review and resolve the issue.

Sponsored by the China National Sports Association: Sports Discussion Meeting Opened Yesterday in Qingdao; Zhang Boling Advocates That Promoting Compulsory Education Must Focus on Sports; Hao Gengsheng Speaks on the Prospects of Sports Administration in Our Country

(Qingdao, 29th) The National Sports Discussion Meeting was held at 8:00 AM on the 29th in the auditorium of Shandong University. Chairman Zhang Boling delivered the opening speech, addressing the purpose and methods of the discussion meeting. He then began to present a paper. Hao Gengsheng's presentation was on the prospects of sports administration in our country, and he made three points: (1) Enrich the content of local sports committees; (2) Implement social sports testing; (3) Promote sports exams to achieve the goal of popularizing sports. Following this, Li Zhongsan Zhang Jiwu presented his article on how to define the goals of sports in our country. Then, Zhang Boling was invited to give a public speech. Based on his 30 years of experience in sports and education, he believed that in order to make the nation strong, one should start with developing people. He hoped that sports educators would pay attention to fostering a spirit of cooperation, and that the government's promotion of compulsory education should not be separated from sports, but rather that sports and education should be equally emphasized in order to achieve the goal.

Education News

Ministry of Finance Stops Fujian from Collecting Education Surtax on Skin Silk Tobacco

(Nanjing, 29th) The Shanghai Skin Silk Tobacco Industry Association presented to the Ministry of Finance requesting an order to stop the Fujian Provincial Government from heavily levying an education surtax on skin silk tobacco. The Ministry of Finance has consulted the Fujian Provincial Government to abolish the education surtax, and all education expenses in the province will be subsidized by the Ministry with a monthly allocation of 110,000 yuan.

Members of the Medical Education Committee Appointed: First Meeting in Mid-Next Month

(Nanjing, 29th) After the regulations of the Medical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education were revised, the members of the committee, in addition to Huang Jianzhong and Gu Shusen appointed by the Ministry of Education, and Xin Baoshan and Zhu Zhanggeng appointed by the Ministry of Health, were also hired by the Ministry of Education to appoint Yan Fuqing and seven others as members, and Lin Kesheng and five others were hired as consultants. The first meeting of the committee is scheduled to be held in mid-August.

Round Trip to Beijing Student Settlement Fee: Approved for Over 4,900 Yuan

(Nanjing, 29th) The settlement fee for Xinjiang students returning to Beijing, amounting to 4,944 yuan, has been approved by the Directorate General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics for disbursement from the first reserve fund item of the 24th year of the Republic of China education and culture expenses. The National Government has recently ordered the two courts of the Political Supervision to transfer the order to the three ministries of Finance, Education, and Auditing, as well as the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission.

Ministry of Education Long-Distance Senior Staff

(Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education intends to promote Xie Shuying, section chief of the Higher Education Department, to the position of supervising inspector, and appoint Xue Quan and Gui Liangjie as section chiefs. The nominations were submitted to the Executive Yuan on the 29th and then to the National Government for appointment.

Sichuan Education Department Announces Principals of Provincial and County Middle Schools

(Chongqing, 29th) In order to reorganize the schools in Sichuan Province, the Education Department recently announced the principals of various provincial and county schools, including: Song Dalu, Provincial First Normal School; Zhang Pengxiang, Provincial Third Normal School; Long Bangjun, Provincial Fourth Normal School; Du Zhida, Chengdu Boys' Middle School; Wu Zhaohua, Chengdu Girls' Middle School; Zhang Youfang, Provincial Third Middle School; Shu Xiangsheng, Provincial Fourth Middle School; Yang Jiwu, Provincial Sixth Middle School; Ye Desheng, Chengdu Affiliated Middle School; Lu Shinian, Huayang Middle School; Zhou Zigao, Provincial First Women's Normal School; Zhang Zhongchi, Yan Gao Vocational School; Hu Shuying, Provincial Women's Vocational School; Jiang Bingxing, Jialing High School; Shi Yunde, Leshan Middle School; Zhu Zijiequ, Rongchang Middle School; Yang Dagang, County Middle School; Wang Feng, Dazu Middle School; Song Yuliang, Jiangjin Women's Middle School.

Fujian Children's Year Opens on the 1st

(Fuzhou, 29th) The Provincial Children's Year Implementation Committee invited related agencies to hold a preparatory meeting at the Provincial Party Headquarters on the 29th. The Children's Year opening ceremony will be held at the Literary and Artistic Theater on August 1st, along with a children's amusement fair and a children's music car parade.

Hangzhou Children's Year Opening Postponed: Held in September

The Executive Yuan decided that August 1, 24th year of the Republic of China, would be the start date for Children's Year and stipulated that an opening ceremony should be held when Children's Year begins. The Zhejiang Provincial Children's Year opening ceremony was planned to be held jointly with Hangzhou City. Director Xu of the Provincial Education Department and Mayor Zhou of Hangzhou City specifically invited Committee Member Fang Qingru of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Committee Member Chen Wen of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Section Chief Luo Dixian of the Education Department, and Section Chief Chen Chengren of Hangzhou City to discuss everything at the Education Department on the afternoon of the 26th. As a result of the discussion, it was argued that the opening ceremony should be held on a grand scale. The original date of the opening ceremony was August 1st, but since the elementary schools are not yet in session at this time, and the weather has been hot recently, for the sake of the children's well-being, it was decided to postpone it to September.

The Children's Year in this city is scheduled to open on August 1st. Preparatory Situation The Preparatory Committee for the Opening Ceremony held its final meeting yesterday. (2) It is estimated that 500 students will participate, and the Education Bureau has instructed various schools to send them. 200 child laborers have been instructed by the Social Affairs Bureau to send them from various factories, and 300 poor children have been contacted by Wang Zhenchang from various institutions. Social Activities (1) All stores selling children's items in this city will reduce prices by one day to benefit children. (4) When eating, chew carefully and swallow slowly; (5) Do not eat too many snacks; (6) Do not eat uncooked food; (7) Do not eat spoiled food; (8) Food should not be too hot or too cold; (9) Wash hands before eating; (10) Do not engage in strenuous exercise before or after eating; (11) Eat some fruit after meals to aid digestion; (12) Take a walk after meals to promote health; (13) Brush teeth after meals; (14) Wash face after meals; (3) Children's bedding should be washed and changed frequently; (4) Children should sleep for ten hours each day; (5) Children should sleep alone; (6) Children should not engage in strenuous exercise before going to bed; (7) Children should develop the habit of going to bed early and waking up early; (8) Children should not drink too much tea or eat too much food before going to bed; (4) Walking Aspect: (1) Walk on the left side; (2) Do not jump or run around while walking; (3) Walk with light steps; (4) Do not look around while walking; (5) Pay attention to front, back, left, and right while walking; (6) Do not rush while walking; (5) Health Aspect: (1) Check children's physical condition twice a year; (2) Children should be vaccinated against smallpox twice a year to prevent the spread of smallpox; (3) Children should often go to the wilderness to take walks and play games to improve their personal health; (4) Satisfy children's healthy life; (5) Pay attention to the development of children's physical and mental health; (6) Improve midwifery; (7) Implement scientific childcare methods; (8) Children should have appropriate exercise; (9) Save children first in case of danger; (10) Only healthy children can have a strong nation; (6) Education Aspect: (1) Do not use harsh methods to educate children; (2) Pay special attention to the selection of children's reading materials; (3) Children should not read reading materials with bad content; (4) Children should not read reading materials with too small fonts; (5) Children should not read reading materials with glossy paper; (6) Children's reading time should not be too long; (7) Children must have a good reading environment; (8) It is a great honor to raise good children; (9) Teachers should patiently guide children; (10) Infant care knowledge is essential for young women; (11) Make special children's education films; (12) Parents' words and actions are the norms for their children; (13) Good children are the result of good family education; (14) Develop children's education; (15) Maternal education is the element for achieving great people; (16) To make the country prosperous, we must first pay attention to children's education; (2) Entertainment Aspect: (1) There must be sufficient time every day to entertain children's body and mind; (2) Proper entertainment can promote children's health; (3) Establish special children's parks; (4) Watch beneficial children's movies; (5) Schools and families should purchase children's toys as much as possible; (6) Tell jokes from time to time; (7) Natural life is the sweetest statistic that children love; (8) Singing is a good way to cultivate temperament.

Six Organizations' Annual Meeting in Guizhou: Members from Various Places Depart in Batches; Gathering on the 7th in Wuzhou, Guangxi University; Wu Lien-te Did Not Join Due to Traveling Abroad

The joint annual meeting of six academic organizations, including the Science Society of China, is scheduled to be held in Nanning, Guizhou Province, starting on August 11th. Previous reports have covered various details. Now, we have learned that members from Shanghai and other places have already departed in batches. The details are as follows:

Departure of Members for the Joint Annual Meeting

Members of the six organizations—the Science Society of China, the Chemical Society, the Geographical Society, the Zoological Society, and the Botanical Society—are departing in batches on ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the Taikoo Dockyard & Engineering Company, and others from Shanghai to Guangzhou due to the imminent joint annual meeting. From there, they will transfer to Wuzhou. Members from the northwestern provinces have also departed from Hankou by train on the Wuchang-Changsha Railway, traveling overland to Guangzhou. They are scheduled to gather at Guangxi University in Wuzhou on the 7th, and then take a special vessel provided by the provincial government to Nanning. They are expected to arrive by the 10th. It is reported that reception centers have been set up in Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Wuzhou, and Nanning, so long-distance travel should be without difficulty.

Wu Lien-te Scheduled to Travel Abroad on the 1st

Wu Lien-te, a director of the Science Society of China, was originally scheduled to attend the joint annual meeting. However, the Second Pacific International Health Conference will be held in Australia, and Wu has been appointed by the Health Department to attend. Therefore, he did not join the group. Wu is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the Dutch Royal Mail Line's "Zeester" on August 1st. He is carrying several proposals that he intends to present for discussion at the conference and report on the health facilities in our country.

Guangzhou Municipal Government Decides to Host

The Guangzhou Municipal Government has decided to host a reception for the attendees of the annual meeting when they arrive in Guangzhou on their way back after the meeting. The itinerary has been decided as follows: A joint banquet in the city at 7:00 PM on August 23rd; visits to sugar and alcohol factories on the morning of the 24th, sightseeing in the afternoon, and a banquet hosted by the provincial government in the evening; visits to cement, tap water, new electricity, and fertilizer factories on the morning of the 25th, a public banquet at Sun Yat-sen University at noon, and a visit to a textile factory in the afternoon, followed by a public banquet hosted by the municipal government at 7:00 PM.

Introducing "Little Men"

— Gan

A New Contribution to the Opening of Children's Year in This Newspaper

To be Published in This Column Starting August 1st

The Famous Work of Ms. Louisa May Alcott of the United States

Translated by Zheng Xiaocang, Director of the Department of Education at Zhejiang University

There are three prerequisites for implementing children's education: first, excellent teachers; second, perfect teaching materials; and third, a loving society. Only when all three are in place can the implementation of children's education be easy and effective. Among the three, the selection of children's teaching materials is the most important, because it has a great impact on the development of children's intelligence.

Our newspaper has always taken the promotion of children's education as its mission. In October of the year before last, we launched "Children's Weekly." In this year's Children's Day, we published "Children's Friend." All publications aim to make a small contribution in terms of children's teaching materials. Now, on the occasion of the opening of Children's Year, we have specially commissioned Mr. Zheng Xiaocang to translate the book "Little Men." The author of this book, Ms. Louisa May Alcott, is the daughter of the American philosopher Bronson Alcott. She devoted her life to education and writing, enduring many hardships but never changing her ambition. After the publication of "Little Women" and "Good Wives," her reputation soared. The extent of their circulation was unprecedented in the publishing industry. The term "Little Women" is almost a household name in England and the United States. Two years later, she completed the book "Little Men." On the day of its publication, the author had just returned to the United States from Europe. Friends greeted her in a carriage with a red banner inscribed with the three characters "Little Men," hanging high above the port. It is said that pre-orders for this book in the United States had reached more than 50,000 copies before its publication, which can be considered a great success.

This book describes more than a dozen boys and girls with different temperaments, who live a free and unrestrained life under proper supervision, so that their bodies become healthier and their knowledge gradually improves. All their actions are full of educational meaning, with guidance embedded in suggestion. It is truly a good book for teachers, parents, and children. As for the vividness of its writing, anyone who has read "Little Women" and "Good Wives" can predict it. Moreover, the translator, Mr. Zheng, is known to the country for his learning and experience in education and literature. His translations of Alcott's books are fluent and accessible, and have been widely praised. Now he has translated this famous work, which will surely be even more successful. Then we are even more willing to use the name of the translator to add a layer of guarantee to this book.

Commercial News

Finance: Ceaseless Buying Pressure; Gold Market Breaks Through the 90 Yuan Barrier; Higher Than the Closing Price by More Than 21 Yuan; Result of Competitive Bidding is a Sharp Increase of 10 Yuan

Yesterday, the gold market was up. Although foreign banks reversed their earlier gains and declined, investor sentiment remained bullish. Banks were eager to cover their short positions, and the domestic market was extremely tight. Major players were aggressively buying, creating a short squeeze in the market. The market broke through the 90 yuan barrier. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw London rise and New York remain flat. The forward silver price in Montreux was unchanged or up by a small fraction. Exchange rates narrowed slightly, and the price of spot gold in London fell by a penny, slightly dampening investor enthusiasm. In pre-market trading, the price opened lower at 68.89 yuan. Buyers became active at the lower prices, and the price soon rebounded to 70.12 yuan. The Central Bank's announced rates were flat for both the British pound and the US dollar. The customs gold unit narrowed by a fraction, and the benchmark gold price retreated to 871.7 yuan before recovering slightly. The market opened lower in the morning, but buying was eager after the opening, and the price trended upward. However, some banks took advantage of the high prices to sell, and there was some pullback. The anticipated announcement of the HSBC rates showed the British pound and the US dollar to be flat, and the price of domestic goods rose slightly. The situation remained stable, investor sentiment was bullish, and the foreign exchange market was tightening and trending upward. Banks took advantage of the high prices to sell, and the Hong Kong market eased, with some pullback. However, the supply was scarce, buying was extremely strong, and banks were reluctant to sell large amounts. The domestic market continued to tighten, and major players quickly bought. The price surged, breaking through the 80 yuan barrier. Banks were eager to cover their short positions, further strengthening the trend. Later, some major players sold off and then bought back. Silver futures forecasts indicated a contraction of three annas, but the market remained stable. The afternoon close showed a continued upward trend, and buying momentum showed no signs of weakening. The outlook was for the Hong Kong market to weaken, and the HSBC rates were revised downward, contracting the British pound by 0.25 and the US dollar by 0.5. Investor sentiment was again bullish, and pre-market trading rose from 4 yuan to 9 yuan. Major players then began to supply, and the price fell slightly. Trading was stable after the opening, and although there was some upward movement, there were also many pullbacks. However, banks were eager to cover their short positions, and the Chinese Merchants Bank also had an appetite. The domestic market was bullish, and the Hong Kong market followed suit. Major players bought aggressively, and some sold foreign exchange, converting it into futures contracts. A short squeeze then developed in the market, and rumors abounded. The price broke through the 90 yuan barrier, and the upward trend intensified. Later, as the banks' willingness to cover their short positions slowed, major players began to bid to sell. The silver futures report had not yet been received, and the price retreated to within the 90 yuan barrier, experiencing a temporary weakness. However, short sellers continued to cover, and there was a lack of supply. The price soon broke through the 90 yuan barrier again, and the market remained bullish at the end of the day. The day's market situation was unusually bullish, the supply was tight, and the upward trend seemed difficult to stop. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

Yesterday, the 29th, was the delivery date for July futures public bonds on the Chinese Securities Exchange. Although it was after the Hebei Incident and under pressure from various circumstances, with difficult internal and external affairs and numerous hurdles, those preparing to receive goods were still very enthusiastic. The delivery volume for July still reached 43.39 million. Among this, after various brokers offset long and short positions and settled independently, 19.66 million were settled. Those settled on the exchange amounted to 14.13 million. The number of off-exchange settlements was even higher than this. Therefore, on the surface, it seemed as though people were selling off due to the worsening environment. However, since the North China Incident, the unsoundness of the financial circles in Tianjin and Shanghai, coupled with the massive floods, has been increasingly alarming. Bears took advantage of this to resist stubbornly, but as a result, various merchants became increasingly unsure of where to invest. With industry in decline and the silver and money business difficult to develop, various speculative funds gradually concentrated in the public bond market. On July 11, there were disturbances in Tianjin, and rumors of a reduction in bond interest rates spread in the market, causing extreme panic. At the time, salt tax bonds fell by 7.4 yuan, troop disbandment bonds fell by 7.75 yuan, and gold short bonds fell by 9.1 yuan. Later, after the rumors subsided and the Hebei Incident was resolved, the market initially rebounded due to the bears covering their positions, followed by purchases by retail investors and large investors switching from short to long positions, causing prices to rise. Finally, as the July futures period was nearing its end, there were sudden rumors of gold and pound loans, and even talk of banks reducing the cash portion of their paper money reserves from 60% to 40%, intensifying concerns about currency inflation, causing prices to surge sharply, coming within only 3 yuan or so of the high prices on May 30. However, currently, people's confidence remains strong, and it is not easy to see a sudden small decline. The 96 public bond has been able to stand independently and rise firmly amidst the tumultuous waves in various bond markets, entirely due to the support of a certain group. Its future is not entirely unfavorable. The July futures delivery accounts and total trading volumes are listed separately below (unit: 100 yuan).
